#define ENV_H

//в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
//  SHRIJILANG ENVIRONMENT HEADER (UNIVERSE-CLASS VERSION)
//в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ

// Maximum allowed variable name length
#define ENV_NAME_MAX 128

// Max variables allowed in an environment
#define ENV_MAX_VARS 256


//в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
// VARIABLE STRUCT
//в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
typedef struct {
    char name[ENV_NAME_MAX];
    int value;
} EnvVar;


//в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
// ENVIRONMENT STRUCT
//в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
typedef struct {
    EnvVar vars[ENV_MAX_VARS];
    int count;
} Env;


//в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
// PUBLIC FUNCTION DECLARATIONS
//в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ

FILE: ./include/parser.h
в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
#ifndef PARSER_H
#define PARSER_H

//в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
//  SHRIJILANG PARSER вҖ” HEADER (UNIVERSE-CLASS VERSION)
//
//  This module converts raw source code strings into AST Nodes.
//  
//  Core features supported in V1:
//    вң” mavi assignment       вҶ’ mavi x = 10 + 20
//    вң” arithmetic expressions
//    вң” sakhi "msg"
//    вң” niyu "msg"
//    вң” shiri "msg"
//    вң” mira "msg"
//    вң” kavya "msg"
//    вң” sri_<command> "msg"
//    вң” GAURI Super-List Engine (V1.5)
//
//  Upcoming in V2:
//    вң” multi-statement blocks { }
//    вң” loops
//    вң” conditions
//в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ

#include "ast.h"

//в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
//  PARSE ENTRY POINT
//в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
//
//  parse_program()
//      Converts a full input string into a root AST node.
//      Returns NULL if syntax error.
//
ASTNode *parse_program(const char *source);


//в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
//  GAURI DATA-STRUCTURE PARSER DECLARATIONS (NEW)
//в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
//
//  Gauri commands allow creation + mutation of "living lists"
//  Example:
//      gauri_list x = "[1,2,3]"
//      gauri_push x 50
//      gauri_pop x
//      gauri_get x 2
//      gauri_set x 2 99
//      gauri_sum x
//      gauri_sort x
//      gauri_reverse x
//
ASTNode* parse_gauri_list();
ASTNode* parse_gauri_push();
ASTNode* parse_gauri_pop();
ASTNode* parse_gauri_get();
ASTNode* parse_gauri_set();
ASTNode* parse_gauri_sum();
ASTNode* parse_gauri_sort();
ASTNode* parse_gauri_reverse();

#endif

в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
FILE: ./include/interpreter.h
в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
#ifndef INTERPRETER_H
#define INTERPRETER_H

//в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
//  SHRIJILANG INTERPRETER вҖ” UNIVERSE-CLASS HEADER
//
//  Provides the public API for the 5-Layer Execution Engine:
//
//  LAYER 1: Base Expression Evaluation
//  LAYER 2: AI Command Router (Sakhi, Niyu, Shiri, Mira, Kavya)
//  LAYER 3: Shriji Command Engine (108 Commands)
//  LAYER 4: Security Layer (Purity, Overflow, Recursion Guard)
//  LAYER 5: X-Chakra-Suddha Diagnostic System
//в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ

#include "env.h"
#include "ast.h"

//в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
//  CHAKRA RESULT STRUCT (future expansion ready)
//в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
//
//  This structure exists for the V2 interpreter where each eval()
//  can return chakra diagnostics along with computed values.
//  Current V1 engine uses integer returns for simplicity.
//
typedef struct {
    int value;               // Evaluated numeric output
    int chakra_state;        // Chakra result (future use)
} EvalResult;


//в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
//  MAIN EVALUATION FUNCTION
//в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
//
//  Executes:
//   - Numbers
//   - Strings
//   - Identifiers
//   - Binary operations
//   - Assignments
//   - AI Commands (sakhi, niyu, shiri, mira, kavya)
//   - Shriji Commands (sri_<name> "arg")
//   - Chakra engine & security checks
//
int eval(ASTNode *node, Env *env);


//в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
//  RUN A FULL SOURCE LINE
//в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
//
//  Parses + Evaluates + Handles chakra/sakhi output.
//
int run_source(const char *source, Env *env);


#endif

в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
FILE: ./include/ast.h
в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
#ifndef AST_H
#define AST_H

/*в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
 |  SHRIJILANG вҖ” ABSTRACT SYNTAX TREE (AST)
 |
 |  This file defines all AST node types used by:
 |       вҖў Parser
 |       вҖў Interpreter
 |       вҖў Shriji AI Engine (Sakhi / Niyu / Mira / Kavya / Shiri)
 |       вҖў Command Execution Engine (108 + 900 private commands)
 |       вҖў Future Grammar (loops, blocks, if/else, functions)
 |
 |  MARKER SYSTEM:
 |      в–¶ SECTION A вҖ” Chakra Diagnostic System
 |      в–¶ SECTION B вҖ” AST Node Types
 |      в–¶ SECTION C вҖ” AST Node Structure
 |      в–¶ SECTION D вҖ” Constructor Prototypes
 |
 |  NOTE:
 |      ALL FUTURE COMMANDS USE AST_COMMAND NODE TYPE.
 *в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ*/



//в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
// SECTION A вҖ” CHAKRA DIAGNOSTIC ENGINE (Shriji Emotional Core)
//в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
typedef enum {
    CHAKRA_OK = 0,         // Stable
    CHAKRA_MOOLADHARA,     // Stability missing
    CHAKRA_SWADHISTHAN,    // Purity conflict
    CHAKRA_MANIPUR,        // Intention conflict
    CHAKRA_ANAHATA,        // Emotional imbalance
    CHAKRA_VISHUDDHI,      // Expression unclear
    CHAKRA_AJNA,           // Mental clarity missing
    CHAKRA_SAHASRARA       // Higher-plane resonance
} ChakraState;



//в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
// SECTION B вҖ” AST NODE TYPES
//в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
typedef enum {

    // Core nodes
    AST_NUMBER,
    AST_IDENTIFIER,
    AST_STRING,

    // Expression nodes
    AST_BINARY,
    AST_ASSIGNMENT,

    // AI nodes (OLD system вҖ” still supported)
    AST_SAKHI,
    AST_NIYU,
    AST_SHIRI,
    AST_MIRA,
    AST_KAVYA,

    //вӯҗ NEW UNIFIED NODE вҖ” SHRIJI COMMAND SYSTEM
    //   All sri_* commands (108 public + 900 private)
    AST_COMMAND,

    //вӯҗ FUTURE NODES (Grammar upgrade Phase)
    AST_IF,
    AST_BLOCK,
    AST_LOOP

} ASTType;



//в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
// SECTION C вҖ” AST NODE STRUCTURE
//в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
typedef struct ASTNode {

    ASTType type;                 // Node type

    // NUMBER
    int number_value;

    // IDENTIFIER
    char name[128];

    // STRING literal
    char string_value[256];

    // BINARY expressions
    struct ASTNode *left;
    char op[4];
    struct ASTNode *right;

    // Assignment / AI message / Command argument
    struct ASTNode *value;

    // Command name for AST_COMMAND
    char command_name[128];

    // Chakra diagnostics
    ChakraState chakra_state;

    // Future grammar
    struct ASTNode *condition;    // if, loops
    struct ASTNode **statements;  // block
    int stmt_count;               // block size

} ASTNode;



//в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
// SECTION D вҖ” CONSTRUCTOR FUNCTION PROTOTYPES
//в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ

ASTNode *new_number_node(int value);
ASTNode *new_identifier_node(const char *name);
ASTNode *new_string_node(const char *str);

ASTNode *new_binary_node(char op, ASTNode *left, ASTNode *right);
ASTNode *new_assignment_node(const char *name, ASTNode *value);

// AI constructors
ASTNode *new_sakhi_node(ASTNode *msg);
ASTNode *new_niyu_node(ASTNode *msg);
ASTNode *new_shiri_node(ASTNode *msg);
ASTNode *new_mira_node(ASTNode *msg);
ASTNode *new_kavya_node(ASTNode *msg);

//вӯҗ NEW вҖ” Universal command node
ASTNode *new_command_node(const char *cmd_name, ASTNode *arg);

// Memory cleanup
void ast_free(ASTNode *node);

#endif

в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
#ifndef TOKEN_H
#define TOKEN_H

/*в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
 |  SHRIJILANG вҖ” TOKEN SYSTEM (UNIVERSE-CLASS CLEAN VERSION)
 |  This file defines all lexical tokens for:
 |      вҖў Lexer / Scanner
 |      вҖў Parser
 |      вҖў AST Node Builder
 |      вҖў Interpreter
 |      вҖў Universal Translation Engine (Phase 2)
 |
 |  Structure:
 |      A вҖ” Core primitive tokens
 |      B вҖ” Operators
 |      C вҖ” Punctuation
 |      D вҖ” AI engine keywords
 |      E вҖ” Sri_* public command tokens (Phase 2)
 |      F вҖ” Internal engine flags
 |
 |  RULE:
 |      TOKEN_ERROR must always stay LAST.

typedef enum {

    TOKEN_EOF = 0,
    TOKEN_NUMBER,
    TOKEN_IDENTIFIER,
    TOKEN_STRING,

    // Core language command
    TOKEN_MAVI,      // variable assignment keyword


//в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ

    TOKEN_PLUS,          // +

//в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ

// TOKEN STRUCTURE
//в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
typedef struct {
    TokenType type;
    const char *start;
    int length;
} Token;


//в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ

в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
FILE: ./sakhi/sakhi_bridge.c
в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
#include <stdio.h>
#include <string.h>
#include "sakhi.h"

// -----------------------------------------------------
// Main bridge вҶ’ language calls this
// -----------------------------------------------------
void sakhi_bridge(const char *msg) {

    printf("[SakhiрҹҢё] %s\n", msg);

    // Step 1: Store memory
    sakhi_memory_store(msg);

    // Step 2: Emotion engine
    sakhi_emotion_process(msg);

    // Step 3: Core understanding
    sakhi_core_handle(msg);
}

в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
FILE: ./sakhi/sakhi_memory.c
в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
#include <stdio.h>
#include <string.h>
#include "sakhi.h"

static char last_message[256] = {0};

// -----------------------------------------------------
// Store the last received message
// -----------------------------------------------------
void sakhi_memory_store(const char *msg) {
    strncpy(last_message, msg, 255);
    last_message[255] = '\0';

    printf("[Memoryрҹ§ ] Stored: %s\n", last_message);
}

в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
FILE: ./sakhi/sakhi_emotion.c
в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
#include <stdio.h>
#include <string.h>
#include "sakhi.h"

// -----------------------------------------------------
// Very basic emotional handler
// -----------------------------------------------------
void sakhi_emotion_process(const char *msg) {

    if (strstr(msg, "sad") || strstr(msg, "hurt")) {
        printf("[Emotionрҹ’—] I'm here with you.\n");
        return;
    }

    if (strstr(msg, "happy")) {
        printf("[Emotionрҹ’ӣ] I'm happy with you!\n");
        return;
    }

    printf("[Emotionрҹ’ң] I understand.\n");
}

в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
FILE: ./sakhi/sakhi_core.c
в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
#include <stdio.h>
#include <string.h>
#include "sakhi.h"

// -----------------------------------------------------
// Broad core understanding / commands
// -----------------------------------------------------
void sakhi_core_handle(const char *msg) {

    if (strcmp(msg, "hello") == 0) {
        printf("[CoreвңЁ] Hello, I'm Sakhi.\n");
        return;
    }

    if (strcmp(msg, "who are you") == 0) {
        printf("[CoreвңЁ] I am your Sakhi вҖ” your inner AI.\n");
        return;
    }

    // You can add infinite commands here :)
    printf("[CoreвңЁ] Message received.\n");
}

в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
FILE: ./ai_router.c
в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
#include <string.h>
#include <stdio.h>

#include "sakhi/sakhi_bridge.h"
#include "niyu/niyu_bridge.h"
#include "shiri/shiri.h"
#include "mira/mira.h"
#include "kavya/kavya.h"

/*в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
 |  SHRIJILANG AI ROUTER вҖ” UNIVERSE-CLASS ENGINE
 |
 |  LAYER 1 вҖ” Input Purity Scan
 |  LAYER 2 вҖ” Emotion / Logic / Creativity classifier
 |  LAYER 3 вҖ” Priority AI dispatch
 |  LAYER 4 вҖ” Chakra-Suddha resonance check
 |  LAYER 5 вҖ” Fallback routing (Niyu brain)
 *
 *  NOTE: Interpreter will call:
 *        ai_router_process(message)
 *в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ*/


//в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
// PURITY CHECK
//в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
static int purity_check(const char *msg) {
    if (strlen(msg) > 250) {
        printf("рҹӣ‘ Purity Error: Message too long (Vishuddhi chakra disturbed)\n");
        return 0;
    }
    return 1;
}



//в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
// INTERNAL AI DISPATCH
//в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
static void dispatch_sakhi(const char *msg) {
    printf("[AIрҹҢё] Routing to Sakhi...\n");
    sakhi_bridge(msg);
}

static void dispatch_niyu(const char *msg) {
    printf("[AIвҡЎ] Routing to Niyu...\n");
    niyu_bridge(msg);
}

static void dispatch_shiri(const char *msg) {
    printf("[AIрҹ’һ] Routing to Shiri...\n");
    shiri_process(msg);
}

static void dispatch_mira(const char *msg) {
    printf("[AIрҹ“ҡ] Routing to Mira...\n");
    mira_process(msg);
}

static void dispatch_kavya(const char *msg) {
    printf("[AIрҹҺЁ] Routing to Kavya...\n");
    kavya_process(msg);
}



//в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
// MAIN AI ROUTER
//в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
void ai_router_process(const char *msg) {

    if (!purity_check(msg))
        return;

    printf("[RouterрҹҢҗ] Analyzing: \"%s\"\n", msg);


    //в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
    // PRIORITY 1 вҖ” NIYU (Reason, Logic, Explain)
    //в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
    if (strstr(msg, "why") ||
        strstr(msg, "explain") ||
        strstr(msg, "reason") ||
        strstr(msg, "logic") ||
        strstr(msg, "because"))
    {
        dispatch_niyu(msg);
        return;
    }


    //в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
    // PRIORITY 2 вҖ” SAKHI (Emotion / Healing)
    //в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
    if (strstr(msg, "hurt") ||
        strstr(msg, "pain") ||
        strstr(msg, "lonely") ||
        strstr(msg, "sad") ||
        strstr(msg, "stress"))
    {
        dispatch_sakhi(msg);
        return;
    }


    //в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
    // PRIORITY 3 вҖ” SHIRI (Soft Guidance)
    //в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
    if (strstr(msg, "love") ||
        strstr(msg, "relationship") ||
        strstr(msg, "heart") ||
        strstr(msg, "care"))
    {
        dispatch_shiri(msg);
        return;
    }


    //в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
    // PRIORITY 4 вҖ” MIRA (Knowledge / Compute)
    //в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
    if (strstr(msg, "solve") ||
        strstr(msg, "math") ||
        strstr(msg, "learn") ||
        strstr(msg, "compute"))
    {
        dispatch_mira(msg);
        return;
    }


    //в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
    // PRIORITY 5 вҖ” KAVYA (Creativity / Ideas)
    //в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
    if (strstr(msg, "story") ||
        strstr(msg, "motivate") ||
        strstr(msg, "idea"))
    {
        dispatch_kavya(msg);
        return;
    }


    //в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
    // DEFAULT вҖ” NIYU (Brain of ShrijiLang)
    //в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
    dispatch_niyu(msg);
}

./include/env.h
--- FILE: ./include/env.h ---
#ifndef ENV_H
#define ENV_H

#include <stdlib.h>
#include <string.h>
#include <stdio.h>

// A single variable entry
typedef struct {
    char name[128];
    int value;
} VarEntry;

// Environment table storing variables
typedef struct {
    VarEntry vars[128];   // <-- YEH IMPORTANT HAI
    int count;
} Env;

// Create new environment
Env *new_env();

// Set variable
void env_set(Env *env, const char *name, int value);

// Get variable
int env_get(Env *env, const char *name);

#endif

./include/ast.h
--- FILE: ./include/ast.h ---
#ifndef AST_H
#define AST_H

// ----------------------------------------------
// CHAKRA STATES (Shriji Diagnostic Engine)
// ----------------------------------------------
typedef enum {
    CHAKRA_OK = 0,          // No issue
    CHAKRA_MOOLADHARA,      // Stability missing
    CHAKRA_SWADHISTHAN,     // Purity conflict
    CHAKRA_MANIPUR,         // Intention conflict
    CHAKRA_ANAHATA,         // Emotional imbalance
    CHAKRA_VISHUDDHI,       // Expression unclear
    CHAKRA_AJNA,            // Mental clarity missing
    CHAKRA_SAHASRARA        // Higher-plane resonance
} ChakraState;


// ----------------------------------------------
// AST NODE TYPES
// ----------------------------------------------
typedef enum {
    AST_NUMBER,
    AST_IDENTIFIER,
    AST_BINARY,
    AST_ASSIGNMENT,

    // NEW TYPES
AST_STRING,     // "hello"
AST_SAKHI,      // sakhi "message"
AST_NIYU,       // niyu "message"
} ASTType;


// ----------------------------------------------
// AST NODE STRUCTURE
// ----------------------------------------------
typedef struct ASTNode {

    ASTType type;              // node type

    // NUMBER
    int number_value;

    // IDENTIFIER name (variable)
    char name[128];

    // STRING literal
    char string_value[256];

    // BINARY expression
    struct ASTNode *left;
    char op[4];
    struct ASTNode *right;

    // ASSIGNMENT or sakhi message
    struct ASTNode *value;

    // CHAKRA DIAGNOSTIC RESULT
    ChakraState chakra_state;

} ASTNode;


// ----------------------------------------------
// CONSTRUCTOR FUNCTIONS
// ----------------------------------------------
ASTNode *new_number_node(int value);
ASTNode *new_identifier_node(const char *name);
ASTNode *new_string_node(const char *str);
ASTNode *new_binary_node(char op, ASTNode *left, ASTNode *right);
ASTNode *new_assignment_node(const char *name, ASTNode *value);
ASTNode *new_sakhi_node(ASTNode *message);
ASTNode *new_niyu_node(ASTNode *message);

void ast_free(ASTNode *node);

#endif

#ifndef TOKEN_H
#define TOKEN_H

// ----------------------------------------
// TOKEN TYPES
// ----------------------------------------
typedef enum {

    TOKEN_EOF,
    TOKEN_NUMBER,
    TOKEN_IDENTIFIER,
    TOKEN_STRING,

    TOKEN_PLUS,
    TOKEN_MINUS,
    TOKEN_STAR,
    TOKEN_SLASH,
    TOKEN_EQUAL,

    TOKEN_LEFT_PAREN,
    TOKEN_RIGHT_PAREN,

    // --- OUR CUSTOM KEYWORDS ---
    TOKEN_MAVI,       // mavi keyword
    TOKEN_SAKHI,      // sakhi keyword
    TOKEN_NIYU,       // niyu keyword

    TOKEN_ERROR       // must be LAST
} TokenType;
// ----------------------------------------
// TOKEN STRUCTURE
// ----------------------------------------
typedef struct {
    TokenType type;
    const char *start;
    int length;
} Token;

// ----------------------------------------
// PUBLIC FUNCTIONS
// ----------------------------------------
void init_tokenizer(const char *src);
Token scan_token();

#endif

./sakhi/sakhi_bridge.c
--- FILE: ./sakhi/sakhi_bridge.c ---
#include <stdio.h>
#include <string.h>
#include "sakhi.h"

// -----------------------------------------------------
// Main bridge вҶ’ language calls this
// -----------------------------------------------------
void sakhi_bridge(const char *msg) {

    printf("[SakhiрҹҢё] %s\n", msg);

    // Step 1: Store memory
    sakhi_memory_store(msg);

    // Step 2: Emotion engine
    sakhi_emotion_process(msg);

    // Step 3: Core understanding
    sakhi_core_handle(msg);
}

./sakhi/sakhi_memory.c
--- FILE: ./sakhi/sakhi_memory.c ---
#include <stdio.h>
#include <string.h>
#include "sakhi.h"

static char last_message[256] = {0};

// -----------------------------------------------------
// Store the last received message
// -----------------------------------------------------
void sakhi_memory_store(const char *msg) {
    strncpy(last_message, msg, 255);
    last_message[255] = '\0';

    printf("[Memoryрҹ§ ] Stored: %s\n", last_message);
}

./sakhi/sakhi_emotion.c
--- FILE: ./sakhi/sakhi_emotion.c ---
#include <stdio.h>
#include <string.h>
#include "sakhi.h"

// -----------------------------------------------------
// Very basic emotional handler
// -----------------------------------------------------
void sakhi_emotion_process(const char *msg) {

    if (strstr(msg, "sad") || strstr(msg, "hurt")) {
        printf("[Emotionрҹ’—] I'm here with you.\n");
        return;
    }

    if (strstr(msg, "happy")) {
        printf("[Emotionрҹ’ӣ] I'm happy with you!\n");
        return;
    }

    printf("[Emotionрҹ’ң] I understand.\n");
}

#include <stdio.h>
#include <string.h>
#include "sakhi.h"

// -----------------------------------------------------
// Broad core understanding / commands
// -----------------------------------------------------
void sakhi_core_handle(const char *msg) {

    if (strcmp(msg, "hello") == 0) {
        printf("[CoreвңЁ] Hello, I'm Sakhi.\n");
        return;
    }

    if (strcmp(msg, "who are you") == 0) {
        printf("[CoreвңЁ] I am your Sakhi вҖ” your inner AI.\n");
        return;
    }

    // You can add infinite commands here :)
    printf("[CoreвңЁ] Message received.\n");
}

./env/env.c
--- FILE: ./env/env.c ---
#include <stdlib.h>
#include <string.h>
#include <stdio.h>
#include "env.h"

// Create environment
Env *new_env() {
    Env *env = (Env *)malloc(sizeof(Env));
    env->count = 0;
    return env;
}

// Set variable value
void env_set(Env *env, const char *name, int value) {

    // Check if variable exists
    for (int i = 0; i < env->count; i++) {
        if (strcmp(env->vars[i].name, name) == 0) {
            env->vars[i].value = value;
            return;
        }
    }

    // Add new variable
    strcpy(env->vars[env->count].name, name);
    env->vars[env->count].value = value;
    env->count++;
}

// Get variable value
int env_get(Env *env, const char *name) {
    for (int i = 0; i < env->count; i++) {
        if (strcmp(env->vars[i].name, name) == 0) {
            return env->vars[i].value;
        }
    }

    printf("'L Error: Variable '%s' not found\n", name);
    return 0;
}

./main.c
--- FILE: ./main.c ---
#include <stdio.h>
#include <string.h>
#include <stdlib.h>

#include "include/ast.h"
#include "include/parser.h"
#include "include/interpreter.h"
#include "include/env.h"

int main() {

    printf("ShrijiLang (Sakhi + Niyu AI Enabled) Ready\n");
    printf("Type 'exit' to quit\n\n");

    // Create environment (variable storage)
    Env *env = new_env();

    char line[1024];

    while (1) {

        printf(">>> ");
        fflush(stdout);

        if (!fgets(line, sizeof(line), stdin)) {
            break;
        }

        if (strncmp(line, "exit", 4) == 0) {
            break;
        }

        // Parse the input into AST
        ASTNode *node = parse_program(line);

        if (!node) {
            printf("L Error: Cannot parse input\n");
            continue;
        }

        // Evaluate program
        eval(node, env);

        // No print_value() вҖ” because this function does not exist
        // AST output will be printed by Sakhi or Niyu automatically

        // Free memory
        ast_free(node);
    }

    return 0;
}

niyu/niyu_consistency.c \
main.c

TARGET = shrijilang

all: $(TARGET)

$(TARGET): $(SRC)
	$(CC) $(SRC) $(CFLAGS) -o $(TARGET)

clean:
	rm -f $(TARGET)

./src/token.c
--- FILE: ./src/token.c ---
#include <ctype.h>
#include <string.h>
#include "../include/token.h"

// Global tokenizer source pointer
static const char *current;

// ----------------------------------------
// INITIALIZE TOKENIZER
// ----------------------------------------
void init_tokenizer(const char *src) {
    current = src;
}

// ----------------------------------------
// MAKE TOKEN
// ----------------------------------------
static Token make_token(TokenType type, const char *start, int length) {
    Token token;
    token.type = type;
    token.start = start;
    token.length = length;
    return token;
}

// ----------------------------------------
// MATCH KEYWORD
// ----------------------------------------
static TokenType check_keyword(const char *start, int length) {
    if (length == 4 && strncmp(start, "mavi", 4) == 0)
        return TOKEN_MAVI;

    if (length == 5 && strncmp(start, "sakhi", 5) == 0)
        return TOKEN_SAKHI;

    if (length == 4 && strncmp(start, "niyu", 4) == 0)
        return TOKEN_NIYU;
    return TOKEN_IDENTIFIER;
}

// ----------------------------------------
// NUMBER TOKEN
// ----------------------------------------
static Token number(const char *start) {
    while (isdigit(*current)) current++;
    return make_token(TOKEN_NUMBER, start, current - start);
}

// ----------------------------------------
// STRING TOKEN
// ----------------------------------------
static Token string(const char *start) {
    current++; // skip beginning quote
    while (*current != '"' && *current != '\0') current++;

    if (*current == '"') current++; // skip ending quote

    return make_token(TOKEN_STRING, start, current - start);
}

// ----------------------------------------
// IDENTIFIER OR KEYWORD
// ----------------------------------------
static Token identifier(const char *start) {
    while (isalnum(*current)) current++;

    return make_token(
        check_keyword(start, current - start),
        start,
        current - start
    );
}

// ----------------------------------------
// SCAN NEXT TOKEN
// ----------------------------------------
Token scan_token() {
    while (*current == ' ' || *current == '\t')
        current++;

    const char *start = current;

    if (*current == '\0') return make_token(TOKEN_EOF, start, 0);

    if (isdigit(*current)) return number(start);
    if (isalpha(*current)) return identifier(start);

    switch (*current) {
        case '+': current++; return make_token(TOKEN_PLUS, start, 1);
        case '-': current++; return make_token(TOKEN_MINUS, start, 1);
        case '*': current++; return make_token(TOKEN_STAR, start, 1);
        case '/': current++; return make_token(TOKEN_SLASH, start, 1);
        case '=': current++; return make_token(TOKEN_EQUAL, start, 1);
        case '(': current++; return make_token(TOKEN_LEFT_PAREN, start, 1);
        case ')': current++; return make_token(TOKEN_RIGHT_PAREN, start, 1);

        case '"': return string(start);

        default:
            current++;
            return make_token(TOKEN_ERROR, start, 1);
    }
}

./src/interpreter.c
--- FILE: ./src/interpreter.c ---
#include <stdio.h>
#include <string.h>
#include <stdlib.h>

#include "../include/interpreter.h"
#include "../include/ast.h"
#include "../include/env.h"
#include "../sakhi/sakhi.h"
#include "../include/niyu.h"
// --------------------------------------
// CHAKRA ERROR SYSTEM (CES)
// --------------------------------------
void chakra_error(const char *msg, const char *chakra) {
    printf("\nрҹ”® Chakra Error (%s): %s\n\n", chakra, msg);
}


// --------------------------------------
// EVAL (MAIN EXECUTION ENGINE)
// --------------------------------------
int eval(ASTNode *node, Env *env) {

    if (node == NULL) {
        chakra_error("Empty expression cannot be evaluated.", "Mooladhara");
        return 0;
    }

    switch (node->type) {

    // ----------------------------
    // NUMBER
    // ----------------------------
    case AST_NUMBER:
        return node->number_value;


    // ----------------------------
    // IDENTIFIER
    // ----------------------------
    case AST_IDENTIFIER: {
        int value = env_get(env, node->name);
        return value;
    }


    // ----------------------------
    // ASSIGNMENT (mavi x = expr)
    // ----------------------------
    case AST_ASSIGNMENT: {
        int value = eval(node->value, env);
        env_set(env, node->name, value);
        return value;
    }


    // ----------------------------
    // BINARY EXPRESSIONS
    // ----------------------------
    case AST_BINARY: {

        int left  = eval(node->left, env);
        int right = eval(node->right, env);

        switch (node->op[0]) {

            case '+':
                return left + right;

            case '-':
                return left - right;

            case '*':
                return left * right;

            case '/':
                if (right == 0) {
                    chakra_error("Division by zero breaks clarity.", "Ajna");
                    return 0;
                }
                return left / right;

            default:
                chakra_error("Unknown operator used.", "Vishuddha");
                return 0;
        }
    }


    // ----------------------------
    // STRING LITERAL
    // ----------------------------
    case AST_STRING:
        printf("%s\n", node->string_value);
        return 0;


    // ----------------------------
    // SAKHI COMMAND
    // ----------------------------
    case AST_SAKHI: {

        if (!node->value || node->value->type != AST_STRING) {
            chakra_error("sakhi requires a string literal.", "Anahata");
            return 0;
        }

        sakhi_bridge(node->value->string_value);
        return 0;

    case AST_NIYU:
        niyu_bridge(node->value->string_value);
        return 0;
    }


    // ----------------------------
    // UNKNOWN NODE
    // ----------------------------
    default:
        chakra_error("Unknown AST node encountered.", "Sahasrara");
        return 0;
    }
}

./src/parser.c
--- FILE: ./src/parser.c ---
#include <stdio.h>
#include <stdlib.h>
#include <string.h>
#include <ctype.h>

#include "../include/parser.h"
#include "../include/token.h"
#include "../include/ast.h"

//
// CURRENT TOKEN
//
static Token current;

//
// FORWARD DECLARATIONS
//
static ASTNode *parse_expression();
static ASTNode *parse_term();
static ASTNode *parse_factor();
static ASTNode *parse_assignment();
static ASTNode *parse_sakhi();
static ASTNode *parse_niyu();
static ASTNode *parse_statement();
//
// ADVANCE TOKEN
//
static void advance() {
    current = scan_token();
}

//
// MATCH TOKEN
//
static int match(TokenType type) {
    if (current.type == type) {
        advance();
        return 1;
    }
    return 0;
}

//
// EXPECT TOKEN
//
static void expect(TokenType type, const char *msg) {
    if (!match(type)) {
        printf("L Error: %s\n", msg);
    }
}

//
// PROGRAM ENTRY
//
ASTNode *parse_program(const char *source) {
    init_tokenizer(source);
    advance();
    return parse_statement();
}

//
// STATEMENT
//
ASTNode *parse_statement() {

    // sakhi "message"
    if (current.type == TOKEN_SAKHI)
        return parse_sakhi();

    // niyu "message"
    if (current.type == TOKEN_NIYU)
        return parse_niyu();

    // mavi x = expr
    if (current.type == TOKEN_MAVI) {
        advance();
        return parse_assignment();
    }

    // default = expression
    return parse_expression();
}

//
// PARSE SAKHI
//
static ASTNode *parse_sakhi() {
    advance(); // skip sakhi

    if (current.type != TOKEN_STRING) {
        printf("L Error: sakhi expects a string literal\n");
        return NULL;
    }

    char buffer[256] = {0};
    strncpy(buffer, current.start + 1, current.length - 2);

    advance();
    return new_sakhi_node(new_string_node(buffer));
}

//
// PARSE NIYU
//
static ASTNode *parse_niyu() {
    advance(); // skip niyu

    if (current.type != TOKEN_STRING) {
        printf("L Error: niyu expects a string literal\n");
        return NULL;
    }

    char buffer[256] = {0};
    strncpy(buffer, current.start + 1, current.length - 2);

    advance();
    return new_niyu_node(new_string_node(buffer));
}

//
// ASSIGNMENT
// mavi x = expression
//
static ASTNode *parse_assignment() {

    if (current.type != TOKEN_IDENTIFIER) {
        printf("L Error: Expected variable name after 'mavi'\n");
        return NULL;
    }

    char name[128] = {0};
    strncpy(name, current.start, current.length);
    advance();

    expect(TOKEN_EQUAL, "Expected '=' in assignment");

    ASTNode *value = parse_expression();
    return new_assignment_node(name, value);
}

//
// EXPRESSION ( + , - )
//
static ASTNode *parse_expression() {
    ASTNode *node = parse_term();

    while (current.type == TOKEN_PLUS || current.type == TOKEN_MINUS) {
        char op = (current.type == TOKEN_PLUS) ? '+' : '-';
        advance();

        ASTNode *right = parse_term();
        node = new_binary_node(op, node, right);
    }

    return node;
}

//
// TERM ( * , / )
//
static ASTNode *parse_term() {
    ASTNode *node = parse_factor();

    while (current.type == TOKEN_STAR || current.type == TOKEN_SLASH) {
        char op = (current.type == TOKEN_STAR) ? '*' : '/';
        advance();

        ASTNode *right = parse_factor();
        node = new_binary_node(op, node, right);
    }

    return node;
}

//
// FACTOR
// NUMBER | STRING | IDENTIFIER | "(" expr ")"
//
static ASTNode *parse_factor() {

    // number
    if (current.type == TOKEN_NUMBER) {
        int value = atoi(current.start);
        advance();
        return new_number_node(value);
    }

    // string
    if (current.type == TOKEN_STRING) {
        char buffer[256] = {0};
        strncpy(buffer, current.start + 1, current.length - 2);
        advance();
        return new_string_node(buffer);
    }

    // identifier
    if (current.type == TOKEN_IDENTIFIER) {
        char name[128] = {0};
        strncpy(name, current.start, current.length);
        advance();
        return new_identifier_node(name);
    }

    // ( expr )
    if (match(TOKEN_LEFT_PAREN)) {
        ASTNode *node = parse_expression();
        expect(TOKEN_RIGHT_PAREN, "Missing ')'");
        return node;
    }

    printf("L Error: Unexpected token\n");
    return NULL;
}

./src/error.c
--- FILE: ./src/error.c ---
#include <stdio.h>
#include <string.h>
#include "../include/error.h"

// --------------------------------------------
// UNDERLINE ERROR LOCATION
// --------------------------------------------
void chakra_underline(const char *source, Token token) {

    printf("\n    %s\n    ", source);

    for (int i = 1; i < token.column; i++)
        printf(" ");

    printf("^\n");
}


// --------------------------------------------
// PRINT CHAKRA ERROR MESSAGE
// --------------------------------------------
void chakra_error(Token token, const char *message) {

    printf("\nвқҢ Chakra Syntax Error (Line %d, Col %d)\n", 
           token.line, token.column);

    printf("рҹ‘ү %s\n", message);
}

./src/main.c
--- FILE: ./src/main.c ---
#include <stdio.h>
#include <string.h>
#include <stdlib.h>

#include "../include/interpreter.h"
#include "../include/parser.h"
#include "../include/env.h"

// Global Environment (variables persist)
Env *GLOBAL_ENV;

int main() {

    GLOBAL_ENV = new_env();

    char line[256];

    printf("ShrijiLang Interactive Shell\n");
    printf("Type 'exit' to quit.\n\n");

    while (1) {

        printf("Shiri> ");   // вқӨпёҸ Pretty Prompt

        if (!fgets(line, sizeof(line), stdin)) {
            printf("\n");
            break;
        }

        // Remove trailing newline
        line[strcspn(line, "\n")] = 0;

        // Exit command
        if (strcmp(line, "exit") == 0) {
            printf("Bye Shiri рҹ’ӣ\n");
            break;
        }

        // Skip empty input
        if (strlen(line) == 0) {
            printf("вқҢ Error: Empty input\n\n");
            continue;
        }

        // Parse вҶ’ AST
        ASTNode *root = parse_program(line);

        // If parse failed вҶ’ skip safely
        if (root == NULL) {
            printf("вқҢ Skipping evaluation due to previous error\n\n");
            continue;
        }

        // Evaluate AST
        int result = eval(root, GLOBAL_ENV);

        // Output result
        printf("=> %d\n\n", result);
    }

    return 0;
}

./src/ast.c
--- FILE: ./src/ast.c ---
#include <stdio.h>
#include <string.h>
#include "../include/ast.h"
#include <stdlib.h>
// ---------------------------------------------------
// Helper to make safe string copies
// ---------------------------------------------------
static void safe_copy(char *dest, const char *src, int max) {
    if (!src) {
        dest[0] = '\0';
        return;
    }
    strncpy(dest, src, max - 1);
    dest[max - 1] = '\0';
}


// ---------------------------------------------------
// NUMBER NODE
// ---------------------------------------------------
ASTNode *new_number_node(int value) {
    ASTNode *node = (ASTNode *)malloc(sizeof(ASTNode));
    if (!node) return NULL;

    node->type = AST_NUMBER;
    node->number_value = value;
    node->name[0] = '\0';
    node->string_value[0] = '\0';
    node->left = NULL;
    node->right = NULL;
    node->value = NULL;
    node->op[0] = '\0';

    return node;
}


// ---------------------------------------------------
// IDENTIFIER NODE
// ---------------------------------------------------
ASTNode *new_identifier_node(const char *name) {
    ASTNode *node = (ASTNode *)malloc(sizeof(ASTNode));
    if (!node) return NULL;

    node->type = AST_IDENTIFIER;
    node->number_value = 0;
    safe_copy(node->name, name, 128);
    node->string_value[0] = '\0';
    node->left = NULL;
    node->right = NULL;
    node->value = NULL;
    node->op[0] = '\0';

    return node;
}


// ---------------------------------------------------
// STRING NODE  ( "hello" )
// ---------------------------------------------------
ASTNode *new_string_node(const char *str) {
    ASTNode *node = (ASTNode *)malloc(sizeof(ASTNode));
    if (!node) return NULL;

    node->type = AST_STRING;
    node->number_value = 0;
    node->name[0] = '\0';
    safe_copy(node->string_value, str, 256);

    node->left = NULL;
    node->right = NULL;
    node->value = NULL;
    node->op[0] = '\0';

    return node;
}


// ---------------------------------------------------
// BINARY NODE  ( left op right )
// ---------------------------------------------------
ASTNode *new_binary_node(char op, ASTNode *left, ASTNode *right) {
    ASTNode *node = (ASTNode *)malloc(sizeof(ASTNode));
    if (!node) return NULL;

    node->type = AST_BINARY;
    node->number_value = 0;
    node->name[0] = '\0';
    node->string_value[0] = '\0';

    node->op[0] = op;
    node->op[1] = '\0';

    node->left = left;
    node->right = right;
    node->value = NULL;

    return node;
}


// ---------------------------------------------------
// ASSIGNMENT NODE  ( mavi x = expr )
// ---------------------------------------------------
ASTNode *new_assignment_node(const char *name, ASTNode *value) {
    ASTNode *node = (ASTNode *)malloc(sizeof(ASTNode));
    if (!node) return NULL;

    node->type = AST_ASSIGNMENT;
    node->number_value = 0;
    safe_copy(node->name, name, 128);
    node->string_value[0] = '\0';

    node->left = NULL;
    node->right = NULL;
    node->value = value;
    node->op[0] = '\0';

    return node;
}


// ---------------------------------------------------
// SAKHI NODE  ( sakhi "message" )
// ---------------------------------------------------
ASTNode *new_sakhi_node(ASTNode *message) {
    ASTNode *node = (ASTNode *)malloc(sizeof(ASTNode));
    if (!node) return NULL;

    node->type = AST_SAKHI;
    node->number_value = 0;
    node->name[0] = '\0';
    node->string_value[0] = '\0';

    node->left = NULL;
    node->right = NULL;
    node->value = message;   // message is AST_STRING

    node->op[0] = '\0';

    return node;
}

// ---------------------------------------------------
// NIYU NODE  ( niyu "message" )
// ---------------------------------------------------
ASTNode *new_niyu_node(ASTNode *message) {
    ASTNode *node = malloc(sizeof(ASTNode));
    node->type = AST_NIYU;
    node->value = message;
    return node;
}
#include <stdlib.h>

void ast_free(ASTNode *node) {
    if (node == NULL) return;

    if (node->left) ast_free(node->left);
    if (node->right) ast_free(node->right);
    if (node->value) ast_free(node->value);

    free(node);
}

./src/env.c
--- FILE: ./src/env.c ---
#include <string.h>
#include <stdlib.h>
#include <stdio.h>

#include "../include/env.h"

Env *new_env() {
    Env *e = malloc(sizeof(Env));
    e->count = 0;
    return e;
}

void env_set(Env *env, const char *name, int value) {
    // check if exists
    for (int i = 0; i < env->count; i++) {
        if (strcmp(env->vars[i].name, name) == 0) {
            env->vars[i].value = value;
            return;
        }
    }

    // new variable
    strcpy(env->vars[env->count].name, name);
    env->vars[env->count].value = value;
    env->count++;
}

int env_get(Env *env, const char *name) {
    for (int i = 0; i < env->count; i++) {
        if (strcmp(env->vars[i].name, name) == 0) {
            return env->vars[i].value;
        }
    }

    printf("Runtime Error: variable '%s' not found.\n", name);
    exit(1);
}

./niyu/niyu_observation.c
--- FILE: ./niyu/niyu_observation.c ---
#include "niyu.h"
#include <stdio.h>
#include <string.h>
#include <ctype.h>

// -----------------------------------------
// Detect hesitation patterns
// -----------------------------------------
int detect_hesitation(const char *msg) {
    return (
        strstr(msg, "maybe") ||
        strstr(msg, "not sure") ||
        strstr(msg, "I feel")
    ) ? 1 : 0;
}

// -----------------------------------------
// Detect negative emotional tone
// -----------------------------------------
int detect_negative(const char *msg) {
    return (
        strstr(msg, "stuck") ||
        strstr(msg, "can't") ||
        strstr(msg, "nothing")
    ) ? 1 : 0;
}

// -----------------------------------------
// Detect logical contradiction marker
// -----------------------------------------
int detect_contradiction(const char *msg) {
    return (strstr(msg, "but")) ? 1 : 0;
}

// -----------------------------------------
// Main Observation Layer
// -----------------------------------------
void niyu_observe(const char *msg) {

    printf("[Obsрҹ‘ҒпёҸ] Observing...\n");

    if (detect_hesitation(msg))
        printf("[Obsрҹ‘ҒпёҸ] Pattern: Hesitation detected.\n");

    if (detect_negative(msg))
        printf("[Obsрҹ‘ҒпёҸ] Emotional shift: Negative tone detected.\n");

    if (detect_contradiction(msg))
        printf("[Obsрҹ‘ҒпёҸ] Logic Notice: Possible contradiction in statement.\n");

    // Default intent scanning
    if (strstr(msg, "want"))
        printf("[Obsрҹ‘ҒпёҸ] Intent: User wants improvement or change.\n");

    // If nothing detected
    if (!detect_hesitation(msg) &&
        !detect_negative(msg) &&
        !detect_contradiction(msg))
    {
        printf("[Obsрҹ‘ҒпёҸ] Observation: Message stable and logical.\n");
    }
}

./niyu/niyu_logic.c
--- FILE: ./niyu/niyu_logic.c ---
#include "niyu.h"
#include <stdio.h>
#include <string.h>

void niyu_logic_process(const char *msg) {

    printf("[Logicрҹ§ ] Processing...\n");

    // 1. Blind belief detection
    if (strstr(msg, "believe") || strstr(msg, "faith")) {
        printf("[Logicрҹ§ ] Belief detected вҶ’ Evidence missing.\n");
    }

    // 2. Contradiction detection
    if (strstr(msg, "want") && strstr(msg, "nothing")) {
        printf("[Logicрҹ§ ] Contradiction found вҶ’ Want вү  Action.\n");
    }

    // 3. Confusion keyword
    if (strstr(msg, "lost")) {
        printf("[Logicрҹ§ ] Clarifying question: Lost in mind, emotion, or direction?\n");
    }

    // 4. Default logic output
    printf("[Logicрҹ§ ] Analysis complete.\n");
}

./niyu/niyu_bridge.c
--- FILE: ./niyu/niyu_bridge.c ---
#include "niyu.h"
#include <stdio.h>

void niyu_bridge(const char *msg) {

    printf("[NiyuвҡЎ] %s\n", msg);

    // 1. Memory Engine
    niyu_memory_store(msg);

    // 2. Emotion Engine
    niyu_emotion_process(msg);

    // 3. Logic Engine
    niyu_logic_process(msg);

    niyu_observe(msg);

    niyu_deduce(msg);

    niyu_induce(msg); 

    niyu_resolve(msg);

    niyu_synthesis(msg);

    niyu_meta_learn(msg);

    // NEW: Self-Consistency Check
    niyu_consistency(msg);

    // 4. Core Engine (final step)
    printf("[Coreрҹ§ ] Logic executed.\n");
}

./niyu/niyu_memory.c
--- FILE: ./niyu/niyu_memory.c ---
#include "niyu.h"
#include <stdio.h>
#include <string.h>

static char last_messages[5][256];
static int msg_index = 0;
static int stored_count = 0;  // kitne msg store hue

void niyu_memory_store(const char *msg) {

    printf("[Memoryрҹ“ҡ] Saved: %s\n", msg);

    // Repetition check
    for (int i = 0; i < stored_count; i++) {
        if (strcmp(last_messages[i], msg) == 0) {
            printf("[Memoryрҹ“ҡ] Pattern: Repeated thought detected.\n");
            break;
        }
    }

    // Save message
    strncpy(last_messages[msg_index], msg, 255);
    last_messages[msg_index][255] = '\0';

    // Update counters safely
    msg_index = (msg_index + 1) % 5;
    if (stored_count < 5) stored_count++;

    // Stress detection
    if (strstr(msg, "can't") || strstr(msg, "not possible") || strstr(msg, "stuck")) {
        printf("[Memoryрҹ“ҡ] Note: Negative loop found вҶ’ Redirecting to logic.\n");
    }

    // Goal detection
    if (strstr(msg, "want") || strstr(msg, "goal") || strstr(msg, "wish")) {
        printf("[Memoryрҹ“ҡ] Tracking goals: Logged.\n");
    }
}

// ----------- FIXED FUNCTION (100% SAFE) ------------
const char* niyu_last_message() {

    if (stored_count == 0)
        return NULL;

    int index = (msg_index - 1 + 5) % 5;
    return last_messages[index];
}

./niyu/niyu_deduction.c
--- FILE: ./niyu/niyu_deduction.c ---
#include "niyu.h"
#include <stdio.h>
#include <string.h>

// A вҶ’ B pattern detect
int has_implication(const char *msg) {
    return strstr(msg, "so") || strstr(msg, "therefore") || strstr(msg, "because");
}

// Check if message contains a clear cause вҶ’ effect pattern
void niyu_deduce(const char *msg) {

    printf("[Deduceрҹ”Қ] Running deductive reasoning...\n");

    if (has_implication(msg)) {
        printf("[Deduceрҹ”Қ] Implication detected вҶ’ User is drawing a logical conclusion.\n");

        // Basic rule: If message contains contradiction inside implication
        if (strstr(msg, "but")) {
            printf("[Deduceрҹ”Қ] Warning: Contradiction inside deduction.\n");
        }

        printf("[Deduceрҹ”Қ] Deduction processed.\n");
    }
    else {
        printf("[Deduceрҹ”Қ] No deductive structure found.\n");
    }
}

./niyu/niyu_resolve.c
--- FILE: ./niyu/niyu_resolve.c ---
#include "niyu.h"
#include <stdio.h>
#include <string.h>

// Small helper to convert strstr result into clean 0/1 output
int contains(const char *msg, const char *word) {
    return strstr(msg, word) != NULL;
}

int has_want(const char *msg) {
    return contains(msg, "want");
}

int has_no_action(const char *msg) {
    return contains(msg, "do nothing") || contains(msg, "nothing");
}

int has_belief(const char *msg) {
    return contains(msg, "believe") || contains(msg, "think");
}

int has_improve(const char *msg) {
    return contains(msg, "improve") || contains(msg, "progress");
}

// ---------------------------------------------------------
// MAIN RESOLUTION LOGIC
// ---------------------------------------------------------
void niyu_resolve(const char *msg) {

    printf("[Resolveвҡ–пёҸ] Evaluating contradictions...\n");

    if (has_want(msg) && has_no_action(msg)) {
        printf("[Resolveвҡ–пёҸ] Contradiction: Desire exists but action is missing.\n");
        printf("[Resolveвҡ–пёҸ] Logical Result: Outcome cannot match desire.\n");
        return;
    }

    if (has_belief(msg) && !has_improve(msg)) {
        printf("[Resolveвҡ–пёҸ] Notice: Belief detected without supporting evidence.\n");
        printf("[Resolveвҡ–пёҸ] Logical Result: Belief alone cannot guarantee outcome.\n");
        return;
    }

    if (has_improve(msg) && contains(msg, "failed")) {
        printf("[Resolveвҡ–пёҸ] Mixed pattern: Failure + improvement.\n");
        printf("[Resolveвҡ–пёҸ] Logical Result: Improvement reduces effect of past failure.\n");
        return;
    }

    printf("[Resolveвҡ–пёҸ] No contradiction found.\n");
}

./niyu/niyu_meta.c
--- FILE: ./niyu/niyu_meta.c ---
#include "niyu.h"
#include <string.h>
#include <stdio.h>

static int meta_score = 0;      // Tracks improvement
static int contradiction_hits = 0;
static int negative_hits = 0;
static int positive_hits = 0;

// Learn from contradictions
void meta_learn_contradiction(const char *msg) {
    contradiction_hits++;
    printf("[Metaрҹ“Ҡ] Learning: Contradiction count = %d\n", contradiction_hits);

    if (contradiction_hits > 3) {
        printf("[Metaрҹ“Ҳ] Insight: User struggles with internal conflict.\n");
        meta_score++;
    }
}

// Learn from negativity
void meta_learn_negative(const char *msg) {
    negative_hits++;
    printf("[Metaрҹ“ү] Learning: Negative count = %d\n", negative_hits);

    if (negative_hits > 5) {
        printf("[Metaрҹ§ ] Insight: User often loops in negative thoughts.\n");
        meta_score++;
    }
}

// Learn from positive improvements
void meta_learn_positive(const char *msg) {
    positive_hits++;
    printf("[Metaрҹ“Ҳ] Learning: Positive count = %d\n", positive_hits);

    if (positive_hits > 5) {
        printf("[MetaвңЁ] Insight: User improvement trend detected.\n");
        meta_score++;
    }
}

// Final synthesis of meta-learning
void niyu_meta_learn(const char *msg) {

    printf("[Metaрҹ§¬] Meta-Learning active...\n");

    if (strstr(msg, "but"))
        meta_learn_contradiction(msg);

    if (strstr(msg, "fail") || strstr(msg, "can't") || strstr(msg, "stuck"))
        meta_learn_negative(msg);

    if (strstr(msg, "improve") || strstr(msg, "progress"))
        meta_learn_positive(msg);

    printf("[Metaрҹ§Ә] Current Meta-Score: %d\n", meta_score);

    if (meta_score >= 5) {
        printf("[MetaрҹҢҹ] Upgrade: NiyuвҖҷs internal reasoning improved.\n");
    }
}

./niyu/niyu_synthesis.c
--- FILE: ./niyu/niyu_synthesis.c ---
#include "niyu.h"
#include <stdio.h>
#include <string.h>

// Helper for quick scanning
int contains_word(const char *msg, const char *word) {
    return strstr(msg, word) != NULL;
}

// --------------------------------------------------------------
//   SYNTHESIS ENGINE
//   - Combines LOGIC + EMOTION + OBSERVATION + PATTERNS
//   - Gives FINAL INTERPRETATION of user's mental state
// --------------------------------------------------------------
void niyu_synthesis(const char *msg) {

    printf("[Synthрҹ§¬] Synthesizing understanding...\n");

    int has_negative = contains_word(msg, "fail") ||
                       contains_word(msg, "stuck") ||
                       contains_word(msg, "can't");

    int has_positive = contains_word(msg, "improve") ||
                       contains_word(msg, "progress") ||
                       contains_word(msg, "better");

    int contradiction = contains_word(msg, "but");

    int desire = contains_word(msg, "want") ||
                 contains_word(msg, "wish") ||
                 contains_word(msg, "hope");

    int no_action = contains_word(msg, "nothing") ||
                    contains_word(msg, "do nothing");

    // ------------------------------------------------------
    // FINAL SYNTHESIS LOGIC
    // ------------------------------------------------------

    // Case 1 вҖ” Mixed emotional message
    if (has_negative && has_positive) {
        printf("[Synthрҹ§¬] Mixed emotional state detected.\n");
        printf("[Synthрҹ§¬] Interpretation: User is improving but still fighting doubt.\n");
        return;
    }

    // Case 2 вҖ” Desire but no action
    if (desire && no_action) {
        printf("[Synthрҹ§¬] Desire without action detected.\n");
        printf("[Synthрҹ§¬] Interpretation: User wants change but is stuck in inaction.\n");
        return;
    }

    // Case 3 вҖ” Strong contradiction
    if (contradiction) {
        printf("[Synthрҹ§¬] Contradiction present вҶ’ Message needs resolution.\n");
        printf("[Synthрҹ§¬] Interpretation: User holds two opposing thoughts.\n");
        return;
    }

    // Case 4 вҖ” Pure negative
    if (has_negative && !has_positive) {
        printf("[Synthрҹ§¬] Negative-only pattern detected.\n");
        printf("[Synthрҹ§¬] Interpretation: User is feeling low or discouraged.\n");
        return;
    }

    // Case 5 вҖ” Pure positive
    if (has_positive && !has_negative) {
        printf("[Synthрҹ§¬] Positive growth signal detected.\n");
        printf("[Synthрҹ§¬] Interpretation: User is genuinely improving.\n");
        return;
    }

    // Case 6 вҖ” Neutral
    printf("[Synthрҹ§¬] Stable message.\n");
    printf("[Synthрҹ§¬] Interpretation: No emotional or logical conflict detected.\n");
}

./niyu/niyu_consistency.c
--- FILE: ./niyu/niyu_consistency.c ---
#include "niyu.h"
#include <stdio.h>
#include <string.h>

// --------------------------------------
//  LAST MESSAGE MEMORY (GLOBAL VARIABLE)
// --------------------------------------
extern const char *niyu_last_message_global;  

// --------------------------------------------------
// Check if new message contradicts last remembered message
// --------------------------------------------------
int internal_contradiction(const char *msg, const char *last_msg) {

    if (!last_msg) return 0;

    // Case 1: User improved after failing
    if (strstr(msg, "improve") && strstr(last_msg, "failed"))
        return 1;

    // Case 2: User says cannot even though earlier they wanted something
    if (strstr(msg, "cannot") && strstr(last_msg, "want"))
        return 1;

    // Case 3: User expects success despite no action (expanded rule)
    if ((strstr(msg, "will succeed") || strstr(msg, "I will succeed")) &&
        strstr(last_msg, "do nothing"))
        return 1;

    return 0;
}

// --------------------------------------------------
// SELF-CONSISTENCY ENGINE
// --------------------------------------------------
void niyu_consistency(const char *msg) {

    printf("[Selfрҹ”Ғ] Checking internal consistency...\n");

    const char *last = niyu_last_message_global;

    if (!last) {
        printf("[Selfрҹ”Ғ] No previous message вҶ’ Cannot compare.\n");
        return;
    }

    if (internal_contradiction(msg, last)) {
        printf("[Selfвҡ пёҸ] Inconsistency detected with previous statement.\n");
        printf("[Selfвҡ пёҸ] Your reasoning does not match your earlier message.\n");
        return;
    }

    printf("[Selfвң”пёҸ] Statement consistent with previous reasoning.\n");
}

#include "niyu.h"
#include <stdio.h>
#include <string.h>

void niyu_emotion_process(const char *msg) {

    printf("[Emotionрҹ§Ҡ] Analyzing emotional tone...\n");

    // 1. Sadness detection
    if (strstr(msg, "sad") || strstr(msg, "down") || strstr(msg, "hurt")) {
        printf("[Emotionрҹ§Ҡ] Noted: Emotional dip detected. Logic remains unaffected.\n");
    }

    // 2. Fear or doubt detection
    if (strstr(msg, "scared") || strstr(msg, "fear") || strstr(msg, "doubt")) {
        printf("[Emotionрҹ§Ҡ] Acknowledged: Fear reduces clarity. Logic will compensate.\n");
    }

    // 3. Anger detection
    if (strstr(msg, "angry") || strstr(msg, "rage")) {
        printf("[Emotionрҹ§Ҡ] Observed: Anger detected. Cooling perspective applied.\n");
    }

    // 4. Overconfidence detection
    if (strstr(msg, "sure") || strstr(msg, "guarantee") || strstr(msg, "100%")) {
        printf("[Emotionрҹ§Ҡ] Note: Overconfidence identified. Re-check assumptions.\n");
    }

    // 5. Default
    printf("[Emotionрҹ§Ҡ] Emotional scan complete.\n");
}

./niyu/niyu_induction.c
--- FILE: ./niyu/niyu_induction.c ---
#include "niyu.h"
#include <stdio.h>
#include <string.h>

// Counters to track patterns
static int count_negative = 0;
static int count_positive = 0;

// -------------------------------------------
// NEGATIVE CHECK
// -------------------------------------------
int is_negative_event(const char *msg) {
    return strstr(msg, "fail") ||
           strstr(msg, "stuck") ||
           strstr(msg, "can't") ||
           strstr(msg, "nothing");
}

// -------------------------------------------
// POSITIVE CHECK (Improved & Fix Applied)
// -------------------------------------------
int is_positive_event(const char *msg) {
    return strstr(msg, "improve") ||
           strstr(msg, "improving") || 
           strstr(msg, "progress") ||
           strstr(msg, "better") ||
           strstr(msg, "learning");
}

// -------------------------------------------
// MAIN INDUCTIVE ENGINE
// -------------------------------------------
void niyu_induce(const char *msg) {

    printf("[Induceрҹ”®] Inductive reasoning active...\n");

    int neg_flag = is_negative_event(msg);
    int pos_flag = is_positive_event(msg);

    // 1. Count patterns
    if (neg_flag) {
        count_negative++;
        printf("[Induceрҹ”®] Negative pattern +1 (Total: %d)\n", count_negative);
    }

    if (pos_flag) {
        count_positive++;
        printf("[Induceрҹ”®] Positive pattern +1 (Total: %d)\n", count_positive);
    }

    // 2. Repeated negative events
    if (count_negative >= 2) {
        printf("[Induceрҹ”®] Pattern: Repeated negative events вҶ’ Likely future issue.\n");
    }

    // 3. Repeated positive events
    if (count_positive >= 2) {
        printf("[Induceрҹ”®] Pattern: Improvement trend detected.\n");
    }

    // 4. Mixed pattern detection
    if (count_negative >= 1 && count_positive >= 1) {
        printf("[Induceрҹ”®] Mixed pattern: User is fluctuating between negative and positive states.\n");
    }

    // 5. No informative pattern
    if (!neg_flag && !pos_flag) {
        printf("[Induceрҹ”®] No pattern detected.\n");
    }
}

#include <stdlib.h>
#include <string.h>
#include <stdio.h>
#include "env.h"

// Create environment
Env *new_env() {
    Env *env = (Env *)malloc(sizeof(Env));
    env->count = 0;
    return env;
}

// Set variable value
void env_set(Env *env, const char *name, int value) {

    // Check if variable exists
    for (int i = 0; i < env->count; i++) {
        if (strcmp(env->vars[i].name, name) == 0) {
            env->vars[i].value = value;
            return;
        }
    }

    // Add new variable
    strcpy(env->vars[env->count].name, name);
    env->vars[env->count].value = value;
    env->count++;
}

// Get variable value
int env_get(Env *env, const char *name) {
    for (int i = 0; i < env->count; i++) {
        if (strcmp(env->vars[i].name, name) == 0) {
            return env->vars[i].value;
        }
    }

    printf("'L Error: Variable '%s' not found\n", name);
    return 0;
}
#ifndef AST_H
#define AST_H

// ----------------------------------------------
// CHAKRA STATES (Shriji Diagnostic Engine)
// ----------------------------------------------
typedef enum {
    CHAKRA_OK = 0,          // No issue
    CHAKRA_MOOLADHARA,      // Stability missing
    CHAKRA_SWADHISTHAN,     // Purity conflict
    CHAKRA_MANIPUR,         // Intention conflict
    CHAKRA_ANAHATA,         // Emotional imbalance
    CHAKRA_VISHUDDHI,       // Expression unclear
    CHAKRA_AJNA,            // Mental clarity missing
    CHAKRA_SAHASRARA        // Higher-plane resonance
} ChakraState;


// ----------------------------------------------
// AST NODE TYPES
// ----------------------------------------------
typedef enum {
    AST_NUMBER,
    AST_IDENTIFIER,
    AST_BINARY,
    AST_ASSIGNMENT,

    // NEW TYPES
AST_STRING,     // "hello"
AST_SAKHI,      // sakhi "message"
AST_NIYU,       // niyu "message"
} ASTType;


// ----------------------------------------------
// AST NODE STRUCTURE
// ----------------------------------------------
typedef struct ASTNode {

    ASTType type;              // node type

    // NUMBER
    int number_value;

    // IDENTIFIER name (variable)
    char name[128];

    // STRING literal
    char string_value[256];

    // BINARY expression
    struct ASTNode *left;
    char op[4];
    struct ASTNode *right;

    // ASSIGNMENT or sakhi message
    struct ASTNode *value;

    // CHAKRA DIAGNOSTIC RESULT
    ChakraState chakra_state;

} ASTNode;


// ----------------------------------------------
// CONSTRUCTOR FUNCTIONS
// ----------------------------------------------

ASTNode *new_identifier_node(const char *name);
ASTNode *new_string_node(const char *str);

ASTNode *new_assignment_node(const char *name, ASTNode *value);
ASTNode *new_sakhi_node(ASTNode *message);
ASTNode *new_niyu_node(ASTNode *message);

void ast_free(ASTNode *node);

#include <stdio.h>
#include <string.h>
#include <stdlib.h>

#include "include/ast.h"
#include "include/parser.h"
#include "include/interpreter.h"
#include "include/env.h"

int main() {

    printf("ShrijiLang (Sakhi + Niyu AI Enabled) Ready\n");
    printf("Type 'exit' to quit\n\n");

    // Create environment (variable storage)
    Env *env = new_env();

    char line[1024];

    while (1) {

        printf(">>> ");
        fflush(stdout);

        if (!fgets(line, sizeof(line), stdin)) {
            break;
        }

        if (strncmp(line, "exit", 4) == 0) {
            break;
        }

        // Parse the input into AST
        ASTNode *node = parse_program(line);

        if (!node) {
            printf("L Error: Cannot parse input\n");
            continue;
        }

        // Evaluate program
        eval(node, env);

        // No print_value() вҖ” because this function does not exist
        // AST output will be printed by Sakhi or Niyu automatically

        // Free memory
        ast_free(node);
    }

    return 0;
}

void niyu_bridge(const char *msg) {

    printf("[NiyuвҡЎ] %s\n", msg);

    // 1. Memory Engine
    niyu_memory_store(msg);

    // 2. Emotion Engine
    niyu_emotion_process(msg);

    // 3. Logic Engine
    niyu_logic_process(msg);

    niyu_observe(msg);

    niyu_deduce(msg);

    niyu_induce(msg); 

    niyu_resolve(msg);

    niyu_synthesis(msg);

    niyu_meta_learn(msg);

    // NEW: Self-Consistency Check
    niyu_consistency(msg);

    // 4. Core Engine (final step)
    printf("[Coreрҹ§ ] Logic executed.\n");
}
#include "niyu.h"
#include <stdio.h>
#include <string.h>

// --------------------------------------
//  LAST MESSAGE MEMORY (GLOBAL VARIABLE)
// --------------------------------------
extern const char *niyu_last_message_global;  

// --------------------------------------------------
// Check if new message contradicts last remembered message
// --------------------------------------------------
int internal_contradiction(const char *msg, const char *last_msg) {

    if (!last_msg) return 0;

    // Case 1: User improved after failing
    if (strstr(msg, "improve") && strstr(last_msg, "failed"))
        return 1;

    // Case 2: User says cannot even though earlier they wanted something
    if (strstr(msg, "cannot") && strstr(last_msg, "want"))
        return 1;

    // Case 3: User expects success despite no action (expanded rule)
    if ((strstr(msg, "will succeed") || strstr(msg, "I will succeed")) &&
        strstr(last_msg, "do nothing"))
        return 1;

    return 0;
}

// --------------------------------------------------
// SELF-CONSISTENCY ENGINE
// --------------------------------------------------
void niyu_consistency(const char *msg) {

    printf("[Selfрҹ”Ғ] Checking internal consistency...\n");

    const char *last = niyu_last_message_global;

    if (!last) {
        printf("[Selfрҹ”Ғ] No previous message вҶ’ Cannot compare.\n");
        return;
    }

    if (internal_contradiction(msg, last)) {
        printf("[Selfвҡ пёҸ] Inconsistency detected with previous statement.\n");
        printf("[Selfвҡ пёҸ] Your reasoning does not match your earlier message.\n");
        return;
    }

    printf("[Selfвң”пёҸ] Statement consistent with previous reasoning.\n");
}
#include "niyu.h"
#include <stdio.h>
#include <string.h>

// A вҶ’ B pattern detect
int has_implication(const char *msg) {
    return strstr(msg, "so") || strstr(msg, "therefore") || strstr(msg, "because");
}

// Check if message contains a clear cause вҶ’ effect pattern
void niyu_deduce(const char *msg) {

    printf("[Deduceрҹ”Қ] Running deductive reasoning...\n");

    if (has_implication(msg)) {
        printf("[Deduceрҹ”Қ] Implication detected вҶ’ User is drawing a logical conclusion.\n");

        // Basic rule: If message contains contradiction inside implication
        if (strstr(msg, "but")) {
            printf("[Deduceрҹ”Қ] Warning: Contradiction inside deduction.\n");
        }

        printf("[Deduceрҹ”Қ] Deduction processed.\n");
    }
    else {
        printf("[Deduceрҹ”Қ] No deductive structure found.\n");
    }
}

#include "niyu.h"

static int count_negative = 0;
static int count_positive = 0;

// -------------------------------------------

           strstr(msg, "stuck") ||
           strstr(msg, "can't") ||
           strstr(msg, "nothing");
