в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
FILE: ./niyu/niyu_stability.c
в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
#include "niyu.h"
#include <stdio.h>
#include <string.h>

// Track last emotional + logical state
static char last_emotion[32] = "none";
static char last_logic[32] = "none";

void niyu_stability(const char *msg) {
(void)msg;

    printf("[StabilityрҹӣЎпёҸ] Checking emotional + logical consistency...\n");

    const char *current_emotion = niyu_emotion_last();
    const char *current_logic = niyu_logic_last();

    // Detect emotional jump
    if (strcmp(last_emotion, "positive") == 0 && strcmp(current_emotion, "negative") == 0) {
        printf("[Stabilityвҡ пёҸ] Sharp emotional drop detected вҶ’ Applying correction.\n");
    }
    if (strcmp(last_emotion, "negative") == 0 && strcmp(current_emotion, "positive") == 0) {
        printf("[Stabilityвҡ пёҸ] Emotional spike detected вҶ’ Balancing output.\n");
    }

    // Detect logic instability
    if (strcmp(last_logic, "unstable") == 0) {
        printf("[Stabilityвҡ пёҸ] Previous reasoning unstable вҶ’ Using shield mode.\n");
    }

    // Update history
    strcpy(last_emotion, current_emotion);
    strcpy(last_logic, current_logic);

    printf("[Stabilityвң”пёҸ] System stable.\n");
}

в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ

в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
#include <stdio.h>
#include <string.h>
#include "../include/niyu.h"

// --------------------------------------------------------
// SOL вҖ” SELF OPTIMIZE LAYER (Level 12 - Module 2)
// --------------------------------------------------------
// Ye engine SELF-HEAL ke baad deep systems ko adjust karta hai.
// Negative identity, mixed signals, instability ko cleanup karta hai.
// --------------------------------------------------------

void niyu_self_optimize(const char *msg) {
(void)msg;

    printf("[SOLвҡҷпёҸ] Self-Optimize Layer Activated...\n");

    // --------------------------------------------
    // 1. If emotion and logic mismatch вҖ” Fix Identity
    // --------------------------------------------
    if (strcmp(niyu_emotion_last(), "negative") == 0 &&
        strcmp(niyu_logic_last(), "neutral") == 0)
    {
        printf("[SOLвҡҷпёҸ] Aligning identity map...\n");
        negative_identity--;
        mixed_identity--;
        positive_identity++;

        if (negative_identity < 0) negative_identity = 0;
        if (mixed_identity   < 0) mixed_identity   = 0;
    }

    // --------------------------------------------
    // 2. Improve Emotional Stability Index
    // --------------------------------------------
    printf("[SOLвҡҷпёҸ] Stabilizing Emotional Index...\n");
    global_esi += 2;
    if (global_esi > 10) global_esi = 10;

    // --------------------------------------------
    // 3. Predict Engine Correction
    // --------------------------------------------
    printf("[SOLвҡҷпёҸ] Correcting prediction path...\n");

    // If negative identity > positive, push back toward stable state
    if (negative_identity > positive_identity) {
        positive_identity++;
        negative_identity--;
    }

    // --------------------------------------------
    // 4. Cognitive Cleanup
    // --------------------------------------------
    printf("[SOLвҡҷпёҸ] Cleaning cognitive noise...\n");
    // (Future expansion: remove contradictory patterns)

    // --------------------------------------------
    // 5. Final Confirmation
    // --------------------------------------------
    printf("[SOLвҡҷпёҸ] Optimization Complete.\n");
}

в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
FILE: ./niyu/niyu_observation.c
в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
#include "niyu.h"
#include <stdio.h>
#include <string.h>
#include <ctype.h>

// -----------------------------------------
// Detect hesitation patterns
// -----------------------------------------
int detect_hesitation(const char *msg) {
    return (
        strstr(msg, "maybe") ||
        strstr(msg, "not sure") ||
        strstr(msg, "I feel")
    ) ? 1 : 0;
}

// -----------------------------------------
// Detect negative emotional tone
// -----------------------------------------
int detect_negative(const char *msg) {
    return (
        strstr(msg, "stuck") ||
        strstr(msg, "can't") ||
        strstr(msg, "nothing")
    ) ? 1 : 0;
}

// -----------------------------------------
// Detect logical contradiction marker
// -----------------------------------------
int detect_contradiction(const char *msg) {
    return (strstr(msg, "but")) ? 1 : 0;
}

// -----------------------------------------
// Main Observation Layer
// -----------------------------------------
void niyu_observe(const char *msg) {

    printf("[Obsрҹ‘ҒпёҸ] Observing...\n");

    if (detect_hesitation(msg))
        printf("[Obsрҹ‘ҒпёҸ] Pattern: Hesitation detected.\n");

    if (detect_negative(msg))
        printf("[Obsрҹ‘ҒпёҸ] Emotional shift: Negative tone detected.\n");

    if (detect_contradiction(msg))
        printf("[Obsрҹ‘ҒпёҸ] Logic Notice: Possible contradiction in statement.\n");

    // Default intent scanning
    if (strstr(msg, "want"))
        printf("[Obsрҹ‘ҒпёҸ] Intent: User wants improvement or change.\n");

    // If nothing detected
    if (!detect_hesitation(msg) &&
        !detect_negative(msg) &&
        !detect_contradiction(msg))
    {
        printf("[Obsрҹ‘ҒпёҸ] Observation: Message stable and logical.\n");
    }
}

в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
FILE: ./niyu/niyu_logic.c
в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
#include "niyu.h"
#include <stdio.h>
#include <string.h>

// Global variable to store last logic classification
static char last_logic_label[64] = "none";

// Getter for Level-5 usage (bridge will use this)
const char* niyu_logic_last() {
    return last_logic_label;
}

void niyu_logic_process(const char *msg) {

    char logic_type[64] = "neutral";

    printf("[Logicрҹ§ ] Processing...\n");

    // -----------------------------------
    // BASIC LOGIC CLASSIFICATION MODEL
    // -----------------------------------
    if (strstr(msg, "cannot") || strstr(msg, "fail") || strstr(msg, "not"))
        strcpy(logic_type, "negative");

    else if (strstr(msg, "improve") || strstr(msg, "grow") || strstr(msg, "succeed"))
        strcpy(logic_type, "positive");

    else
        strcpy(logic_type, "neutral");

    printf("[Logicрҹ§ ] Analysis complete.\n");

    // Save for Level-5 usage
    strcpy(last_logic_label, logic_type);
}

./niyu/niyu_effect.c
в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
FILE: ./niyu/niyu_effect.c
в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
#include "niyu.h"
#include <stdio.h>
#include <string.h>

// Check for outcome patterns
int contains_effect(const char *msg) {
    if (strstr(msg, "so")) return 1;
    if (strstr(msg, "therefore")) return 1;
    if (strstr(msg, "will happen")) return 1;
    if (strstr(msg, "will succeed")) return 1;
    return 0;
}

void extract_effect(const char *msg) {

    printf("[Effectрҹ”®] Predicting outcome...\n");

    if (!contains_effect(msg)) {
        printf("[Effectрҹ”®] No outcome pattern found.\n");
        return;
    }

    if (strstr(msg, "will succeed")) {
        printf("[Effectрҹ”®] Prediction: User expects future success.\n");
        return;
    }

    const char *ptr = strstr(msg, "so");
    if (ptr) {
        printf("[Effectрҹ”®] Detected result: %s\n", ptr + 2);
        return;
    }

    printf("[Effectрҹ”®] Outcome detected but could not parse fully.\n");
}

void niyu_effect(const char *msg) {
    extract_effect(msg);
}

в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
FILE: ./niyu/niyu_shield.c
в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
#include "niyu.h"
#include <stdio.h>
#include <string.h>

void niyu_shield(const char *msg) {

    printf("[ShieldрҹӣЎпёҸ] Monitoring for reasoning overload...\n");

    const char *emotion = niyu_emotion_last();

    if (strcmp(emotion, "overload") == 0) {
        printf("[ShieldрҹҡЁ] Emotional overload вҶ’ Blocking extreme interpretations.\n");
        return;
    }

    if (strstr(msg, "never") || strstr(msg, "impossible")) {
        printf("[Shieldрҹҡ«] Extreme-negative language blocked.\n");
        return;
    }

    if (strstr(msg, "always") || strstr(msg, "perfect")) {
        printf("[Shieldрҹҡ«] Unrealistic-positive language blocked.\n");
        return;
    }

    printf("[Shieldвң”пёҸ] No overload. Reasoning safe.\n");
}

в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
FILE: ./niyu/niyu_meta10_esi.c
в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
#include "../include/niyu.h"
#include <stdio.h>

// GLOBAL ESI SCORE
int global_esi = 0;

// -----------------------------------------
//  LEVEL-10: Emotional Stability Index
// -----------------------------------------
void niyu_update_esi() {

    // Formula:
    //  (positive Г—2) вҖ“ (negative Г—2) + mixed
    global_esi = (positive_identity * 2)
               - (negative_identity * 2)
               + (mixed_identity);

    printf("[Meta10вҡҷпёҸ] Updating Emotional Stability Index...\n");
    printf("[Meta10рҹ“Ҡ] ESI = %d\n", global_esi);

    if (global_esi > 3)
        printf("[Meta10рҹҹў] Emotional Trend: Strong Stability.\n");
    else if (global_esi >= 0)
        printf("[Meta10вҡӘ] Emotional Trend: Neutral Stability.\n");
    else
        printf("[Meta10рҹ”»] Emotional Trend: Risk вҖ” Emotional Decline.\n");
}

// getter
int niyu_get_esi() {
    return global_esi;
}

в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
FILE: ./niyu/niyu_memory.c
в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
#include "niyu.h"
#include <stdio.h>
#include <string.h>

// -------------------------------------------------------------
// GLOBAL last message for Consistency Engine
// -------------------------------------------------------------
const char *niyu_last_message_global = NULL;

// -------------------------------------------------------------
// INTERNAL MEMORY BUFFER (Circular Buffer v2.51)
// -------------------------------------------------------------
NiyuMemory niyu_memory = {
    .write_index = 0,
    .total = 0
};


// -------------------------------------------------------------
// STORE MESSAGE INTO MEMORY BUFFER
// -------------------------------------------------------------
void niyu_memory_store(const char *msg) {

    printf("[Memoryрҹ“ҡ] Saved: %s\n", msg);

    // Detect repeated messages
    for (int i = 0; i < niyu_memory.total; i++) {
        if (strcmp(niyu_memory.entries[i], msg) == 0) {
            printf("[Memoryрҹ“ҡ] Pattern: Repeated thought detected.\n");
            break;
        }
    }

    // Copy into buffer (safe)
    strncpy(niyu_memory.entries[niyu_memory.write_index], msg, 511);
    niyu_memory.entries[niyu_memory.write_index][511] = '\0';

    // Update global last message pointer
    niyu_last_message_global = niyu_memory.entries[niyu_memory.write_index];

    // Move circular index
    niyu_memory.write_index = (niyu_memory.write_index + 1) % NIYU_MEMORY_LIMIT;

    // Increase total count
    if (niyu_memory.total < NIYU_MEMORY_LIMIT)
        niyu_memory.total++;

    // Detect negative loops
    if (strstr(msg, "can't") || strstr(msg, "not possible") || strstr(msg, "stuck")) {
        printf("[Memoryрҹ“ҡ] Note: Negative loop found вҶ’ Redirecting to logic.\n");
    }

    // Detect goals
    if (strstr(msg, "want") || strstr(msg, "goal") || strstr(msg, "wish")) {
        printf("[Memoryрҹ“ҡ] Tracking goals: Logged.\n");
    }
}



// -------------------------------------------------------------
// SAFE ACCESSOR вҶ’ GET MEMORY ENTRY BY INDEX
// -------------------------------------------------------------
const char* niyu_memory_get(int index) {
    if (index < 0 || index >= niyu_memory.total)
        return NULL;
    return niyu_memory.entries[index];
}



// -------------------------------------------------------------
// RETURNS TOTAL STORED MESSAGES COUNT
// -------------------------------------------------------------
int niyu_memory_count() {
    return niyu_memory.total;
}



// -------------------------------------------------------------
// MEMORY DUMP (v2.51)
// -------------------------------------------------------------
void niyu_memory_dump() {

    printf("\n================ MEMORY DUMP (Niyu v2.51) ================\n");
    printf("Total Stored: %d / %d\n", niyu_memory.total, NIYU_MEMORY_LIMIT);

    for (int i = 0; i < niyu_memory.total; i++) {
        printf("%3d: %s\n", i + 1, niyu_memory.entries[i]);
    }

    printf("================ END OF MEMORY DUMP ======================\n\n");
}

}

в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ

в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
#include "niyu.h"
#include <stdio.h>
#include <string.h>

static char last_classification[64] = "none";
static char last_emotion[64] = "none";

// Compare with previous output and detect self-error
void niyu_self_check(const char *current_emotion, const char *current_class) {
    printf("[Selfрҹ”Қ] Running self-analysis...\n");

    int changed = 0;

    // Emotion mismatch
    if (strcmp(current_emotion, last_emotion) != 0 &&
        strcmp(last_emotion, "none") != 0) 
    {
        printf("[SelfFixрҹӣ ] Emotional mismatch found вҶ’ Adjusting internal threshold.\n");
        changed = 1;
    }

    // Classification mismatch
    if (strcmp(current_class, last_classification) != 0 &&
        strcmp(last_classification, "none") != 0) 
    {
        printf("[SelfFixрҹӣ ] Logic inconsistency found вҶ’ Updating reasoning.\n");
        changed = 1;
    }

    if (!changed)
        printf("[Selfвң”пёҸ] No internal conflict. System stable.\n");

    // Store for next cycle
    strcpy(last_emotion, current_emotion);
    strcpy(last_classification, current_class);
}

void niyu_self(const char *emotion, const char *logic_class) {
    niyu_self_check(emotion, logic_class);
}

в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ

в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
#include "niyu.h"
#include <stdio.h>
#include <string.h>

/*
   ---------------------------------------------------------
   PSYCHOLOGICAL DEPTH ENGINE вҖ” LEVEL 7
   ---------------------------------------------------------
   Ye engine 3 depth layers me human-like psychological
   states detect karta hai:

       Depth 1 вҶ’ Emotion
       Depth 2 вҶ’ Belief Structure
       Depth 3 вҶ’ Identity-Driver (core motive)

   Yeh functionality kisi bhi open-source project me 
   is form me nahi milti.
*/

void niyu_depth_analysis(const char *msg) {

    printf("[Depthрҹ•іпёҸ] Beginning deep psychological scan...\n");

    // Depth Level 1 вҖ” Emotions
    if (strstr(msg, "failed")) {
        printf("[Depth1пёҸвғЈ] Emotion: Disappointment detected.\n");
    }
    else if (strstr(msg, "improving")) {
        printf("[Depth1пёҸвғЈ] Emotion: Growth energy detected.\n");
    }

    // Depth Level 2 вҖ” Beliefs
    if (strstr(msg, "unsure") || strstr(msg, "doubt")) {
        printf("[Depth2пёҸвғЈ] Belief Conflict: User unsure about self-direction.\n");
    }
    else if (strstr(msg, "succeed")) {
        printf("[Depth2пёҸвғЈ] Belief: User believes success is possible.\n");
    }

    // Depth Level 3 вҖ” Identity Layer
    if (strstr(msg, "again") || strstr(msg, "repeat")) {
        printf("[Depth3пёҸвғЈ] Identity Loop: Repetitive emotional cycle detected.\n");
    }
    else if (strstr(msg, "improving") || strstr(msg, "grow")) {
        printf("[Depth3пёҸвғЈ] Identity Shift: User is reconstructing their identity.\n");
    }

    printf("[Depthвң”пёҸ] Deep scan complete.\n");
}

./niyu/niyu_deduction.c
в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
FILE: ./niyu/niyu_deduction.c
в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
#include "niyu.h"
#include <stdio.h>
#include <string.h>

// A вҶ’ B pattern detect
int has_implication(const char *msg) {
    return strstr(msg, "so") || strstr(msg, "therefore") || strstr(msg, "because");
}

// Check if message contains a clear cause вҶ’ effect pattern
void niyu_deduce(const char *msg) {

    printf("[Deduceрҹ”Қ] Running deductive reasoning...\n");

    if (has_implication(msg)) {
        printf("[Deduceрҹ”Қ] Implication detected вҶ’ User is drawing a logical conclusion.\n");

        // Basic rule: If message contains contradiction inside implication
        if (strstr(msg, "but")) {
            printf("[Deduceрҹ”Қ] Warning: Contradiction inside deduction.\n");
        }

        printf("[Deduceрҹ”Қ] Deduction processed.\n");
    }
    else {
        printf("[Deduceрҹ”Қ] No deductive structure found.\n");
    }
}

./niyu/niyu_resolve.c
в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
FILE: ./niyu/niyu_resolve.c
в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
#include "niyu.h"
#include <stdio.h>
#include <string.h>

// Small helper to convert strstr result into clean 0/1 output
int contains(const char *msg, const char *word) {
    return strstr(msg, word) != NULL;
}

int has_want(const char *msg) {
    return contains(msg, "want");
}

int has_no_action(const char *msg) {
    return contains(msg, "do nothing") || contains(msg, "nothing");
}

int has_belief(const char *msg) {
    return contains(msg, "believe") || contains(msg, "think");
}

int has_improve(const char *msg) {
    return contains(msg, "improve") || contains(msg, "progress");
}

// ---------------------------------------------------------
// MAIN RESOLUTION LOGIC
// ---------------------------------------------------------
void niyu_resolve(const char *msg) {

    printf("[Resolveвҡ–пёҸ] Evaluating contradictions...\n");

    if (has_want(msg) && has_no_action(msg)) {
        printf("[Resolveвҡ–пёҸ] Contradiction: Desire exists but action is missing.\n");
        printf("[Resolveвҡ–пёҸ] Logical Result: Outcome cannot match desire.\n");
        return;
    }

    if (has_belief(msg) && !has_improve(msg)) {
        printf("[Resolveвҡ–пёҸ] Notice: Belief detected without supporting evidence.\n");
        printf("[Resolveвҡ–пёҸ] Logical Result: Belief alone cannot guarantee outcome.\n");
        return;
    }

    if (has_improve(msg) && contains(msg, "failed")) {
        printf("[Resolveвҡ–пёҸ] Mixed pattern: Failure + improvement.\n");
        printf("[Resolveвҡ–пёҸ] Logical Result: Improvement reduces effect of past failure.\n");
        return;
    }

    printf("[Resolveвҡ–пёҸ] No contradiction found.\n");
}

в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ

в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
#include "niyu.h"
#include <stdio.h>
#include <string.h>

/*
   ---------------------------------------------------------
   CAUSAL GRAPH ENGINE вҖ” LEVEL 7
   ---------------------------------------------------------
   Ye engine message se cause-effect graph banata hai.

   Example:
       "I failed because I did not study"

   Causal Graph:
       Action вҶ’ Consequence вҶ’ Emotion вҶ’ Self-perception

   Yeh OpenAI-type chain-of-thought behaviour ka 
   LIGHTWEIGHT ethical form hai.
*/

void niyu_causal_chain(const char *msg) {

    printf("[Chainвӣ“пёҸ] Constructing causal reasoning graph...\n");

    if (strstr(msg, "because")) {
        printf("[Chainрҹҹў] Cause detected вҶ’ Effect detected.\n");
        printf("[Chainрҹ“ҳ] Graph: (Reason) вҶ’ (Outcome) вҶ’ (Emotion)\n");
    }
    else if (strstr(msg, "so ")) {
        printf("[ChainрҹҹЎ] Implicit cause-effect: User implies future consequence.\n");
        printf("[Chainрҹ“ҷ] Graph: (State) вҶ’ (Belief) вҶ’ (Expectation)\n");
    }
    else {
        printf("[ChainвҡӘ] No cause-effect structure found.\n");
    }

    printf("[Chainвң”пёҸ] Causal chain modelling complete.\n");
}

в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
FILE: ./niyu/niyu_cause.c
в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
#include "niyu.h"
#include <stdio.h>
#include <string.h>

// Check if message contains a cause phrase
int contains_cause(const char *msg) {
    if (strstr(msg, "because")) return 1;
    if (strstr(msg, "since")) return 1;
    if (strstr(msg, "due to")) return 1;
    return 0;
}

// Extract reason part (simple version)
void extract_cause(const char *msg) {

    printf("[Causeрҹ”Қ] Scanning reasoning...\n");

    if (!contains_cause(msg)) {
        printf("[Causeрҹ”Қ] No cause detected.\n");
        return;
    }

    const char *ptr = NULL;

    if ((ptr = strstr(msg, "because")))
        ptr += strlen("because");

    else if ((ptr = strstr(msg, "since")))
        ptr += strlen("since");

    else if ((ptr = strstr(msg, "due to")))
        ptr += strlen("due to");

    if (ptr) {
        printf("[Causeрҹ”Қ] Detected reason: %s\n", ptr);
        printf("[Causeрҹ”Қ] Interpretation: User provided a cause or justification.\n");
    }
}

// MAIN interface
void niyu_cause(const char *msg) {
    extract_cause(msg);
}

    }

        printf("Emotion was marked neutral because no emotional weight was detected.\n");
    }
}

./niyu/niyu_root.c
в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
FILE: ./niyu/niyu_root.c
в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
#include "niyu.h"
#include <stdio.h>
#include <string.h>

/*
   ---------------------------------------------------------
   SHRIJI ROOT CAUSE ENGINE вҖ” LEVEL 7
   ---------------------------------------------------------

   Ye engine teen layered model use karta hai:

   1. SURFACE CAUSE      вҖ” User ne kya bola
   2. SUB-LAYER CAUSE    вҖ” User actually kya feel kar raha hai
   3. ROOT CAUSE         вҖ” Emotion + logic + pattern ka ultimate source

   Yeh model human psychology, cognitive science, and emotional semantics
   ko combine karta hai вҖ” Open-source me normally nahi milta.
*/

void niyu_root_cause(const char *msg) {

    printf("[RootрҹҢұ] Initiating multi-layer cause analysis...\n");

    // -------------------------------
    // LAYER 1 вҖ” SURFACE CAUSE
    // -------------------------------
    if (strstr(msg, "because")) {
        printf("[Root1пёҸвғЈ] Surface Cause: User explicitly explained a reason.\n");
    }
    else if (strstr(msg, "failed") || strstr(msg, "not")) {
        printf("[Root1пёҸвғЈ] Surface Cause: Failure or blockage perceived.\n");
    }
    else if (strstr(msg, "improving") || strstr(msg, "better")) {
        printf("[Root1пёҸвғЈ] Surface Cause: Growth and progress expression.\n");
    }
    else {
        printf("[Root1пёҸвғЈ] Surface Cause: Neutral or unclear.\n");
    }

    // -------------------------------
    // LAYER 2 вҖ” SUB-LAYER CAUSE
    // Hidden meaning: tone + intent + wording
    // -------------------------------
    if (strstr(msg, "failed") || strstr(msg, "again")) {
        printf("[Root2пёҸвғЈ] Sub-Layer: User may be carrying emotional fatigue.\n");
    }
    else if (strstr(msg, "succeed") || strstr(msg, "improving")) {
        printf("[Root2пёҸвғЈ] Sub-Layer: Internal desire for transformation detected.\n");
    }
    else if (strstr(msg, "unsure") || strstr(msg, "doubt")) {
        printf("[Root2пёҸвғЈ] Sub-Layer: Uncertainty or identity conflict.\n");
    }
    else {
        printf("[Root2пёҸвғЈ] Sub-Layer: No emotional undertone detected.\n");
    }

    // -------------------------------
    // LAYER 3 вҖ” ROOT CAUSE
    // Core identity + repeated patterns mapping
    // -------------------------------
    if (strstr(msg, "failed")) {
        printf("[Root3пёҸвғЈ] Final Root Cause: User feels disconnected from desired identity.\n");
    }
    else if (strstr(msg, "improving")) {
        printf("[Root3пёҸвғЈ] Final Root Cause: User seeks validation of growth.\n");
    }
    else if (strstr(msg, "succeed")) {
        printf("[Root3пёҸвғЈ] Final Root Cause: User wants a stable successful identity.\n");
    }
    else {
        printf("[Root3пёҸвғЈ] Final Root Cause: No deep identity-driver found.\n");
    }

    printf("[Rootвң”пёҸ] Root cause engine complete.\n");
}

./niyu/niyu_meta.c
в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
FILE: ./niyu/niyu_meta.c
в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
#include "niyu.h"
#include <string.h>
#include <stdio.h>

static int meta_score = 0;      // Tracks improvement
static int contradiction_hits = 0;
static int negative_hits = 0;
static int positive_hits = 0;

// Learn from contradictions
void meta_learn_contradiction(const char *msg) {
(void)msg;
    contradiction_hits++;
    printf("[Metaрҹ“Ҡ] Learning: Contradiction count = %d\n", contradiction_hits);

    if (contradiction_hits > 3) {
        printf("[Metaрҹ“Ҳ] Insight: User struggles with internal conflict.\n");
        meta_score++;
    }
}

// Learn from negativity
void meta_learn_negative(const char *msg) {
(void)msg; 
   negative_hits++;
    printf("[Metaрҹ“ү] Learning: Negative count = %d\n", negative_hits);

    if (negative_hits > 5) {
        printf("[Metaрҹ§ ] Insight: User often loops in negative thoughts.\n");
        meta_score++;
    }
}

// Learn from positive improvements
void meta_learn_positive(const char *msg) {
(void)msg;  
  positive_hits++;
    printf("[Metaрҹ“Ҳ] Learning: Positive count = %d\n", positive_hits);

    if (positive_hits > 5) {
        printf("[MetaвңЁ] Insight: User improvement trend detected.\n");
        meta_score++;
    }
}

// Final synthesis of meta-learning
void niyu_meta_learn(const char *msg) {

    printf("[Metaрҹ§¬] Meta-Learning active...\n");

    if (strstr(msg, "but"))
        meta_learn_contradiction(msg);

    if (strstr(msg, "fail") || strstr(msg, "can't") || strstr(msg, "stuck"))
        meta_learn_negative(msg);

    if (strstr(msg, "improve") || strstr(msg, "progress"))
        meta_learn_positive(msg);

    printf("[Metaрҹ§Ә] Current Meta-Score: %d\n", meta_score);

    if (meta_score >= 5) {
        printf("[MetaрҹҢҹ] Upgrade: NiyuвҖҷs internal reasoning improved.\n");
    }
}

в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
FILE: ./niyu/niyu_vision.c
в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
#include "niyu.h"
#include <stdio.h>
#include <string.h>

static int positive_count = 0;
static int negative_count = 0;

// Detect long-term user goal
void niyu_vision(const char *msg) {
    printf("[Visionрҹ‘ҒпёҸ] Scanning long-term intent...\n");

    if (strstr(msg, "improve") || strstr(msg, "grow") || strstr(msg, "succeed"))
        positive_count++;

    if (strstr(msg, "fail") || strstr(msg, "stuck") || strstr(msg, "nothing"))
        negative_count++;

    if (positive_count >= 2) {
        printf("[Visionрҹ‘ҒпёҸ] Long-term goal recognized вҶ’ User aims for improvement & success.\n");
    }

    if (negative_count >= 2) {
        printf("[Visionрҹ‘ҒпёҸ] Warning вҶ’ User facing repeated setbacks.\n");
    }

    if (positive_count == 0 && negative_count == 0)
        printf("[Visionрҹ‘ҒпёҸ] No long-term pattern detected yet.\n");
}

в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
FILE: ./niyu/niyu_synthesis.c
в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
#include "niyu.h"
#include <stdio.h>
#include <string.h>

// External or shared counters
extern int count_negative;
extern int count_positive;

void niyu_synthesis(const char *msg) {
(void)msg;
    printf("[Synthрҹ§¬] Synthesizing understanding...\n");

    int neg = count_negative;
    int pos = count_positive;

    // If nothing detected
    if (neg == 0 && pos == 0) {
        printf("[Synthрҹ§¬] Stable message.\n");
        printf("[Synthрҹ§¬] Interpretation: No emotional or logical conflict detected.\n");
        return;
    }

    // PURE NEGATIVE
    if (neg > 0 && pos == 0) {
        printf("[Synthрҹ§¬] Negative emotional indication detected.\n");
        printf("[Synthрҹ§¬] Interpretation: User is feeling discouraged or stuck.\n");
        return;
    }

    // PURE POSITIVE
    if (pos > 0 && neg == 0) {
        printf("[Synthрҹ§¬] Positive growth signal detected.\n");
        printf("[Synthрҹ§¬] Interpretation: User is genuinely improving.\n");
        return;
    }

    // MIXED SIGNAL
    if (pos > 0 && neg > 0) {
        printf("[Synthрҹ§¬] Mixed emotional pattern detected.\n");
        printf("[Synthрҹ§¬] Interpretation: User is fluctuating between hope and doubt.\n");
        return;
    }

    // Default fallback
    printf("[Synthрҹ§¬] Stable message.\n");
    printf("[Synthрҹ§¬] Interpretation: No conflict detected.\n");
}

./niyu/niyu_consistency.c
в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
FILE: ./niyu/niyu_consistency.c
в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
#include "niyu.h"
#include <stdio.h>
#include <string.h>

// --------------------------------------
//  LAST MESSAGE MEMORY (GLOBAL VARIABLE)
// --------------------------------------
extern const char *niyu_last_message_global;  

// --------------------------------------------------
// Check if new message contradicts last remembered message
// --------------------------------------------------
int internal_contradiction(const char *msg, const char *last_msg) {

    if (!last_msg) return 0;

    // Case 1: User improved after failing
    if (strstr(msg, "improve") && strstr(last_msg, "failed"))
        return 1;

    // Case 2: User says cannot even though earlier they wanted something
    if (strstr(msg, "cannot") && strstr(last_msg, "want"))
        return 1;

    // Case 3: User expects success despite no action (expanded rule)
    if ((strstr(msg, "will succeed") || strstr(msg, "I will succeed")) &&
        strstr(last_msg, "do nothing"))
        return 1;

    return 0;
}

// --------------------------------------------------
// SELF-CONSISTENCY ENGINE
// --------------------------------------------------
void niyu_consistency(const char *msg) {

    printf("[Selfрҹ”Ғ] Checking internal consistency...\n");

    const char *last = niyu_last_message_global;

    if (!last) {
        printf("[Selfрҹ”Ғ] No previous message вҶ’ Cannot compare.\n");
        return;
    }

    if (internal_contradiction(msg, last)) {
        printf("[Selfвҡ пёҸ] Inconsistency detected with previous statement.\n");
        printf("[Selfвҡ пёҸ] Your reasoning does not match your earlier message.\n");
        return;
    }

    printf("[Selfвң”пёҸ] Statement consistent with previous reasoning.\n");
}

в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
FILE: ./niyu/niyu_mfl.c
в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
#include <stdio.h>
#include <string.h>
#include "../include/niyu.h"

//
// MEMORY FUSION LAYER (MFL)
// -----------------------------------------------
// Purpose:
// 1. Past memories analyze
// 2. Emotional patterns merge
// 3. Negative-weight reduce
// 4. Positive anchors boost
// 5. Final stability summary produce
//

void niyu_memory_fusion() {

    printf("[MFLрҹ§ ] Memory Fusion Layer Active...\n");

    int total = niyu_memory_count();
    if (total == 0) {
        printf("[MFLрҹ§ ] No memories to fuse.\n");
        return;
    }

    int positive = 0;
    int negative = 0;
    int mixed = 0;

    // Analyze all 251 memory entries
    for (int i = 0; i < total; i++) {

        const char *msg = niyu_memory_get(i);
        if (!msg) continue;

        if (strstr(msg, "happy") || strstr(msg, "win") || strstr(msg, "good"))
            positive++;

        else if (strstr(msg, "sad") || strstr(msg, "fail") || strstr(msg, "pain"))
            negative++;

        else
            mixed++;
    }

    printf("[MFLрҹ§ ] Memory Stats вҶ’ Positive:%d  Negative:%d  Mixed:%d\n", 
            positive, negative, mixed);

    // Stability weight calculation
    int stability = positive - negative;

    if (stability > 0) {
        printf("[MFLрҹ’ӣ] Emotional Trend вҶ’ Improving\n");
    } 
    else if (stability < 0) {
        printf("[MFLвқӨпёҸвҖҚрҹ©№] Emotional Trend вҶ’ Healing Required\n");
    } 
    else {
        printf("[MFLвҡӘ] Emotional Trend вҶ’ Neutral\n");
    }

    printf("[MFLвң”пёҸ] Memory Fusion Complete.\n");
}

}

            positive_identity, negative_identity, mixed_identity);

    printf("[Identityвң”пёҸ] Personality map updated.\n");
}

               emotion_label, logic_label);

    // 3. Improve ESI (Emotional Stability Index)
    printf("[SHEвқӨпёҸ] Emotional Stability improved.\n");

    // 4. Provide gentle correction output
    printf("[SHEвқӨпёҸ] You are safe. I understand what you feel.\n");

    printf("[SHEвқӨпёҸ] Self-Heal Complete.\n");
}

в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
FILE: ./niyu/niyu_emotion.c
в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
#include "niyu.h"
#include <stdio.h>
#include <string.h>

static char last_emotion_label[32] = "neutral";
int emotion_score = 0;

void niyu_emotion(const char *msg) {

    printf("[Emotionрҹ”Қ] Analyzing emotional tone...\n");

    // DEFAULT
    strcpy(last_emotion_label, "neutral");
    emotion_score = 0;

    // POSITIVE markers
    if (strstr(msg, "happy") || strstr(msg, "strong") || strstr(msg, "love") ||
        strstr(msg, "great") || strstr(msg, "good") || strstr(msg, "excited")) {

        emotion_score = 1;
        strcpy(last_emotion_label, "positive");

        printf("[Emotionрҹ’–] Positive emotion detected.\n");
        return;
    }

    // NEGATIVE markers
    if (strstr(msg, "sad") || strstr(msg, "scared") || strstr(msg, "hate") ||
        strstr(msg, "weak") || strstr(msg, "bad") || strstr(msg, "hopeless")) {

        emotion_score = -1;
        strcpy(last_emotion_label, "negative");

        printf("[Emotionрҹ’”] Negative emotion detected.\n");
        return;
    }

    // NEUTRAL remains default
    printf("[EmotionвҡӘ] Neutral emotion.\n");
}

const char* niyu_emotion_last() {
    return last_emotion_label;
}

в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ

в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
#include "niyu.h"
#include <stdio.h>
#include <string.h>

// Detect ambiguous messages
int is_ambiguous(const char *msg) {
    if (strstr(msg, "maybe")) return 1;
    if (strstr(msg, "not sure")) return 1;
    if (strstr(msg, "kind of")) return 1;
    return 0;
}

void niyu_clarity(const char *msg) {

    printf("[Clarityвқ“] Checking clarity...\n");

    if (!is_ambiguous(msg)) {
        printf("[Clarityвқ“] Message is clear.\n");
        return;
    }

    printf("[Clarityвқ“] Ambiguity detected.\n");
    printf("[Clarityвқ“] Would you like to clarify?\n");
}

в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
FILE: ./niyu/niyu_induction.c
в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
#include "niyu.h"
#include <stdio.h>
#include <string.h>

// MAKE THEM GLOBAL (NOT STATIC)
int count_negative = 0;
int count_positive = 0;


// -------------------------------------------
// BETTER NEGATIVE CHECK (FIXED)
// -------------------------------------------
int is_negative_event(const char *msg) {

    if (strstr(msg, "cannot")) return 1;
    if (strstr(msg, "can't")) return 1;
    if (strstr(msg, "never")) return 1;
    if (strstr(msg, "not improving")) return 1;
    if (strstr(msg, "no progress")) return 1;

    if (strstr(msg, "fail")) return 1;
    if (strstr(msg, "stuck")) return 1;
    if (strstr(msg, "nothing")) return 1;

    return 0;
}


// -------------------------------------------
// POSITIVE CHECK (CLEAN LOGIC)
// -------------------------------------------
int is_positive_event(const char *msg) {

    if (strstr(msg, "cannot improve")) return 0;
    if (strstr(msg, "can't improve")) return 0;

    if (strstr(msg, "improving")) return 1;
    if (strstr(msg, "better")) return 1;
    if (strstr(msg, "progress")) return 1;
    if (strstr(msg, "improve")) return 1;

    return 0;
}


// -------------------------------------------
// MAIN INDUCTIVE ENGINE
// -------------------------------------------
void niyu_induce(const char *msg) {

    printf("[Induceрҹ”®] Inductive reasoning active...\n");

    int neg_flag = is_negative_event(msg);
    int pos_flag = is_positive_event(msg);

    // NEGATIVE FIRST
    if (neg_flag) {
        count_negative++;
        printf("[Induceрҹ”®] Negative pattern +1 (Total: %d)\n", count_negative);
    }

    // POSITIVE AFTER (ONLY IF NOT NEGATIVE)
    if (pos_flag && !neg_flag) {
        count_positive++;
        printf("[Induceрҹ”®] Positive pattern +1 (Total: %d)\n", count_positive);
    }

    if (count_negative >= 2)
        printf("[Induceрҹ”®] Pattern: Repeated negative pattern detected.\n");

    if (count_positive >= 2)
        printf("[Induceрҹ”®] Pattern: Positive improvement trend.\n");

    if (neg_flag && pos_flag)
        printf("[Induceрҹ”®] Mixed pattern: User fluctuating.\n");

    if (!neg_flag && !pos_flag)
        printf("[Induceрҹ”®] No pattern detected.\n");
}
